import os
import logging
import datetime
import threading
import stripe
from functools import wraps
from flask import Flask, render_template, jsonify, request, session, redirect, url_for, make_response
from apscheduler.schedulers.background import BackgroundScheduler
import atexit
from firebase_admin import auth as fb_auth

from backend.backend import ThunderData

app = Flask(__name__, static_folder="frontend/static", template_folder="frontend/templates")
app.secret_key = os.environ.get('FLASK_SECRET_KEY', 'gctta-super-secret-session-key')
stripe.api_key = os.environ.get('STRIPE_SECRET_KEY')
app.config['PERMANENT_SESSION_LIFETIME'] = datetime.timedelta(days=30)

logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

db = None
db_lock = threading.Lock()
sync_lock = threading.Lock()
is_first_snapshot = True

def scheduled_refresh():
    global db
    if db and sync_lock.acquire(blocking=False):
        try: 
            logger.info("🔄 Executing background database sync...")
            db.refresh_data()
            logger.info("✅ Background sync complete!")
        except Exception as e: 
            logger.error(f"Background Sync Error: {e}")
        finally:
            sync_lock.release()

def watch_firebase_for_live_matches():
    global db
    if not db or not db.db: return
    
    def on_snapshot(col_snapshot, changes, read_time):
        global is_first_snapshot
        if is_first_snapshot:
            is_first_snapshot = False
            return
            
        has_new_match = False
        for change in changes:
            if change.type.name == 'ADDED':
                has_new_match = True
                
        if has_new_match:
            logger.info("📡 New Match Detected! Triggering Instant Auto-Sync...")
            threading.Thread(target=scheduled_refresh).start()

    try:
        db.db.collection('match_results').where('status', '==', 'approved').on_snapshot(on_snapshot)
        logger.info("📡 Instant Auto-Sync Listener Attached.")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Failed to attach listener: {e}")

@app.before_request
def pre_request_setup():
    global db
    if db is None:
        with db_lock:
            if db is None:
                try:
                    logger.info("Initializing ThunderData safely inside worker process...")
                    db = ThunderData()
                    watch_firebase_for_live_matches()
                    logger.info("✅ Database connected.")
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.error(f"❌ FATAL: Failed to start Backend: {str(e)}")

    if request.path == '/' or request.path == '/index':
        if not request.cookies.get('ghostmode') and not session.get('admin_logged_in'):
            if db:
                ip = request.headers.get('X-Forwarded-For', request.remote_addr)
                if ip: 
                    db.record_page_view(ip.split(',')[0].strip())

scheduler = BackgroundScheduler()
try:
    scheduler.add_job(func=scheduled_refresh, trigger="interval", hours=12, id="scheduled_refresh")
    scheduler.start()
    atexit.register(lambda: scheduler.shutdown())
except Exception as e: pass

def login_required(f):
    @wraps(f)
    def decorated_function(*args, **kwargs):
        if not session.get('admin_logged_in'): return jsonify({'error': 'Unauthorized'}), 401
        return f(*args, **kwargs)
    return decorated_function

def super_admin_required(f):
    @wraps(f)
    def decorated_function(*args, **kwargs):
        role = session.get('admin_role')
        if not session.get('admin_logged_in') or role not in ['super_admin', 'temp_super_admin']: 
            return jsonify({'error': 'Super Admin Required'}), 403
        return f(*args, **kwargs)
    return decorated_function

def verify_player_token(req):
    auth_header = req.headers.get('Authorization')
    if not auth_header or not auth_header.startswith('Bearer '): return None
    token = auth_header.split('Bearer ')[1]
    try:
        decoded = fb_auth.verify_id_token(token)
        return decoded.get('uid')
    except Exception as e:
        return None

@app.route('/ghostmode')
def activate_ghost_mode():
    resp = make_response(jsonify({"success": True, "message": "👻 GHOST MODE ACTIVATED"}))
    resp.set_cookie('ghostmode', '1', max_age=60*60*24*365*10) 
    return resp

@app.route('/')
def index(): return render_template('index.html')
@app.route('/login')
def login(): return redirect(url_for('admin')) if session.get('admin_logged_in') else render_template('login.html')
@app.route('/player_auth')
def player_auth_page(): return render_template('player_auth.html')
@app.route('/dashboard')
def player_dashboard(): return render_template('dashboard.html')

@app.route('/api/auth/google', methods=['POST'])
def auth_google():
    if not db: return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Database offline"})
    user_data = db.verify_admin_token(request.json.get('token'))
    if not user_data: return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Invalid Token"})
        
    if user_data['role'] in ['admin', 'super_admin', 'temp_super_admin']:
        session.permanent = True
        session['admin_logged_in'] = True
        session['admin_email'] = user_data['email']
        session['admin_role'] = user_data['role']
        db._log_audit(user_data['email'], 'SESSION_START', "Admin authenticated and logged in.", {})
        return jsonify({"success": True})
    else: 
        return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Your account is pending approval."})

@app.route('/api/webhook/sms', methods=['POST', 'GET'])
def sms_webhook():
    if not db: return jsonify({"status": "error"}), 500
    try:
        data = request.json if request.is_json else request.form
        sender = data.get('from', 'Unknown')
        body = data.get('body', '')
        if sender and body: db.db.collection('sms_replies').add({'from': sender, 'body': body, 'timestamp': firestore.SERVER_TIMESTAMP, 'status': 'unread'})
        return jsonify({"status": "received"}), 200
    except Exception as e: return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 500

@app.route('/logout')
def logout(): 
    if db and session.get('admin_email'): db._log_audit(session.get('admin_email'), 'SESSION_END', "Admin signed out.", {})
    session.clear()
    return redirect(url_for('index'))

@app.route('/admin')
def admin(): 
    if not session.get('admin_logged_in'): return redirect(url_for('login'))
    return render_template('admin.html', email=session.get('admin_email'), role=session.get('admin_role'))

@app.route('/api/stats/<player_name>')
def get_player_stats(player_name):
    if not db: return jsonify({"error": "Offline"}), 500
    if player_name not in db.all_players:
        for real_name in db.all_players.keys():
            if real_name.lower() == player_name.lower(): 
                player_name = real_name
                break
    stats = db.get_player_stats(player_name, request.args.get('season', 'Career'), request.args.get('division', 'All'))
    if stats: return jsonify(stats)
    return jsonify({"error": "Not found"}), 404

@app.route('/api/create-payment-intent', methods=['POST'])
def create_payment():
    try: 
        amount = int(float(request.json.get('amount', 5.00)) * 100)
        return jsonify({'clientSecret': stripe.PaymentIntent.create(amount=amount, currency='aud', automatic_payment_methods={'enabled': True}).client_secret})
    except Exception as e: return jsonify(error=str(e)), 403

@app.route('/api/admin/upload_schedule', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def upload_schedule():
    if not db: return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "DB Offline"})
    if 'pdf' not in request.files: return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "No file uploaded"})
    season = request.form.get('season', 'Unknown')
    division = request.form.get('division', 'Unknown')
    return jsonify(db.admin_upload_pdf_schedule(season, division, request.files['pdf'], session.get('admin_email')))

@app.route('/api/admin/export_zermelo/<tournament_id>', methods=['GET'])
@login_required
def export_zermelo(tournament_id):
    if not db: return "Offline", 500
    db._log_audit(session.get('admin_email'), 'EXPORT_ZERMELO', f"Downloaded Zermelo CSV for {tournament_id}", {})
    csv_data = db.generate_zermelo_csv(tournament_id)
    if not csv_data: return "Tournament not found", 404
    res = make_response(csv_data)
    res.headers["Content-Disposition"] = f"attachment; filename=zermelo_{tournament_id}.csv"
    res.headers["Content-type"] = "text/csv"
    return res

        p1 = request.json.get('p1')
        p2 = request.json.get('p2')
        db._log_audit(session.get('admin_email'), 'SIMULATOR', f"Ran Glicko match diagnostic on {p1} vs {p2}", {})
        return jsonify({"success": True, "data": db.admin_glicko_math(p1, p2, request.json.get('s1'), request.json.get('s2'))})
    return jsonify({"success": False})

@app.route('/api/admin/send_sms', methods=['POST'])
@login_required
def send_sms():
    if not db: return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Database offline"}), 503
    req_data = request.get_json(silent=True)
    if not req_data or not req_data.get('message'): 
        return jsonify({"success": False, "error": "Message cannot be empty."}), 400
    try:
        return jsonify(db.admin_send_sms_broadcast(req_data.get('message'), req_data.get('phones'), session.get('admin_email'))), 200
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"success": False, "error": f"Internal Server Error: {str(e)}"}), 500

@app.route('/api/hub/tournaments/check_eligibility', methods=['POST'])
def hub_check_eligibility():
    if not db: return jsonify({"eligible": False, "reasons": ["Database offline"]})
    req = request.get_json(silent=True)
    uid = req.get('uid')
    event_data = req.get('event_data', {})
    partner_uid = req.get('partner_uid')
    eligible, reasons = db.check_eligibility(uid, event_data, partner_uid)
    return jsonify({"eligible": eligible, "reasons": reasons})

@app.route('/api/hub/schedule/<player_name>', methods=['GET'])
def get_schedule(player_name): return jsonify(db.get_player_upcoming_schedule(player_name)) if db else jsonify([])
@app.route('/api/hub/tournament/update_cart', methods=['POST'])
def update_cart(): return jsonify(db.process_tournament_cart(request.json.get('uid'), request.json.get('tournament_id'), request.json.get('events'), request.json.get('total'))) if db else jsonify({"success": False})

if __name__ == '__main__':
    port = int(os.environ.get("PORT", 5001))
    app.run(debug=True, host='0.0.0.0', port=port)
==> ./audit.py <==
import gspread
from google.oauth2.service_account import Credentials

# ==========================================
# 👇 SPREADSHEET ID 👇
# ==========================================
SPREADSHEET_ID = "1tpxuUCl8ddpnBBr69vc4P1foRCRKWpts5-HaFPYb4po" 
# ==========================================

# TARGET PLAYER TO DEBUG
TARGET_PLAYER = "Lachlan Cherry"

def run_audit():
    print(f"🕵️ STARTING AUDIT FOR: {TARGET_PLAYER}")
    print("="*60)

    scopes = ["https://www.googleapis.com/auth/spreadsheets"]
    try:
        creds = Credentials.from_service_account_file("backend/credentials.json", scopes=scopes)
    except FileNotFoundError:
        try:
            creds = Credentials.from_service_account_file("credentials.json", scopes=scopes)
        except:
            print("❌ Error: Could not find credentials.json")
            return

    client = gspread.authorize(creds)
    sheet = client.open_by_key(SPREADSHEET_ID)

    total_found = 0
    total_accepted = 0
    
    for worksheet in sheet.worksheets():
        if "Season:" not in worksheet.title:
            continue
            
        print(f"\n📂 Checking Tab: {worksheet.title}")
        records = worksheet.get_all_records()
        
        for i, row in enumerate(records, start=2): # Start at 2 to match Sheet Row numbers
            p1 = str(row.get('Name 1', '')).strip()
            p2 = str(row.get('Name 2', '')).strip()
            
            # Is our guy in this row?
            if TARGET_PLAYER.lower() not in p1.lower() and TARGET_PLAYER.lower() not in p2.lower():
                continue

            total_found += 1
            status = "❓ CHECKING"
            reason = ""
            
            # 1. CHECK FORMAT
            fmt = str(row.get('Format', row.get('Match Format', ''))).lower().strip()
            if "doubles" in fmt:
                print(f"   Row {i}: ❌ SKIPPED (Format is Doubles)")
                continue

            # 2. CHECK SCORES
            s1_raw = row.get('Sets 1')
            s2_raw = row.get('Sets 2')
            
            try:
                if str(s1_raw).strip() == "" or str(s2_raw).strip() == "":
                    print(f"   Row {i}: ❌ SKIPPED (Empty Scores) -> Sets 1: '{s1_raw}', Sets 2: '{s2_raw}'")
                    continue
                
                # Try to convert
                s1 = int(s1_raw)
                s2 = int(s2_raw)
                
                # 3. CHECK FILL-IN STATUS
                ps1 = str(row.get('PS 1', '')).upper()
                ps2 = str(row.get('PS 2', '')).upper()
                
                is_p1 = (TARGET_PLAYER.lower() in p1.lower())
                my_status = ps1 if is_p1 else ps2
                
                type_label = "Fill-in" if my_status == "S" else "Regular"
                
                print(f"   Row {i}: ✅ ACCEPTED as {type_label} | Score: {s1}-{s2} | vs {p2 if is_p1 else p1}")
                total_accepted += 1
                
            except ValueError:
                print(f"   Row {i}: ❌ CRASHED (Bad Score Format) -> Sets 1: '{s1_raw}', Sets 2: '{s2_raw}'")

    print("="*60)
    print(f"AUDIT COMPLETE.")
    print(f"Found {total_found} rows involving {TARGET_PLAYER}.")
    print(f"Successfully loaded {total_accepted} matches.")
    print("="*60)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_audit()

    <script>
        // NEW CROSS-STAR GENERATOR
        function generateStars() {
            const starContainer = document.getElementById('starContainer');
            if(!starContainer) return;
            
            const numberOfStars = 100; // Adjust density as desired
            const colors = ['#ffffff', '#e0f7fa', '#fff9c4', '#bbdefb', '#ffffff']; 

            for (let i = 0; i < numberOfStars; i++) {
                const star = document.createElement('div');
                
                const xPos = Math.random() * 100;
                const yPos = Math.random() * 100;
                // Make the cross shapes slightly larger so they are visible
                const size = Math.random() * 4 + 3; 
                // Randomize speed and massive variations in delay
                const animDuration = Math.random() * 4 + 2; 
                const animDelay = Math.random() * 10; 
                const starColor = colors[Math.floor(Math.random() * colors.length)];

                star.className = 'cross-star';
                star.style.left = `${xPos}vw`;
                star.style.top = `${yPos}vh`;
                star.style.width = `${size}px`;
                star.style.height = `${size}px`;
                star.style.backgroundColor = starColor;
                
                // Attach our custom animation that pauses randomly
                star.style.animation = `sporadic-twinkle ${animDuration}s ease-in-out ${animDelay}s infinite`;

                starContainer.appendChild(star);
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener('popstate', function(event) {
            const reportModal = document.getElementById('reportModal');
            const donateModal = document.getElementById('donateModal');
            const feedbackModal = document.getElementById('feedbackModal');
            const compareModal = document.getElementById('compareModal');
            const matchDetailsModal = document.getElementById('matchDetailsModal');

            if (reportModal && !reportModal.classList.contains('hidden')) { closeReportModal(); return; }
            if (donateModal && !donateModal.classList.contains('hidden')) { closeDonateModal(); return; }
            if (feedbackModal && !feedbackModal.classList.contains('hidden')) { document.getElementById('feedbackModal').classList.add('hidden'); return; }
            if (compareModal && !compareModal.classList.contains('hidden')) { closeCompareModal(); return; }
            if (matchDetailsModal && !matchDetailsModal.classList.contains('hidden')) { closeMatchDetails(); return; }
            
            if (event.state && event.state.tab) { switchTab(event.state.tab, false); }
        });

        window.switchTab = function(tabId, pushHistory = true) {
            if(pushHistory) { history.pushState({ page: 'fixtures', tab: tabId }, "", "#" + tabId); }
            
            // MAP ALL TABS SO THEY PROPERLY HIDE AND SHOW
            ['home', 'week', 'sheets', 'search', 'notices', 'community', 'live-center', 'rules'].forEach(t => { 
                const el = document.getElementById(`tab-${t}`); 
                if(el) el.classList.add('hidden'); 
                const nav = document.getElementById(`nav-${t}`); 
                if(nav) nav.classList.remove('active'); 
                const bnav = document.getElementById(`b-nav-${t}`); 
                if(bnav) bnav.classList.remove('active'); 
            }); 
            
            const stats = document.getElementById('statsContainer'); 
            if(stats) stats.classList.add('hidden'); 
            
            if (tabId === 'statsContainer') { 
                if(stats) { stats.classList.remove('hidden'); stats.classList.add('animate-fade-in'); }
            } else { 
                const target = document.getElementById(`tab-${tabId}`); 
                if(target) { target.classList.remove('hidden'); target.classList.add('animate-fade-in'); } 
                const targetNav = document.getElementById(`nav-${tabId}`); 
                if(targetNav) targetNav.classList.add('active'); 
                const targetBNav = document.getElementById(`b-nav-${tabId}`); 
                if(targetBNav) targetBNav.classList.add('active'); 
                
                if(tabId === 'search') {
                    const searchInput = document.getElementById('bigPlayerSearch');
                    if(searchInput) setTimeout(() => searchInput.focus(), 100);
                }
                
                // AUTO-INITIALIZE COMMUNITY FORUM WHEN CLICKED
                if(tabId === 'community' && typeof window.initCommunity === 'function') {
                    window.initCommunity();
                }
            } 
            window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' }); 
        };

        // FAIL-SAFE: Stop the infinite loading loop if the database is genuinely empty.
        let loadAttempts = 0;
        const originalLoadInitialData = async () => {
            try {
                const pRes = await fetch('/api/players'); 
                window.allPlayersRaw = await pRes.json(); 
                
                if (window.allPlayersRaw.length === 0 && loadAttempts < 10) { 
                    console.log("Waiting for backend background sync to finish...");
                    loadAttempts++;
                    setTimeout(originalLoadInitialData, 3000); 
                    return; 
                }

                setupMainSearch(); 
                const [sRes, dRes] = await Promise.all([fetch('/api/seasons'), fetch('/api/divisions')]);
                const seasons = await sRes.json(); const divisions = await dRes.json();
                
                const latestSeason = seasons.includes("Summer 2026") ? "Summer 2026" : (seasons[seasons.length - 1] || "Career");
                currentSeason = latestSeason;

                const sSelect = document.getElementById('seasonSelect'); if (sSelect) { sSelect.innerHTML = ''; seasons.forEach(s => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = s; opt.innerText = s; sSelect.appendChild(opt); }); sSelect.value = latestSeason; }
                const pDivSelect = document.getElementById('profileDivisionSelect'); if (pDivSelect) { pDivSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="All">All Divisions</option>'; divisions.forEach(d => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = d; opt.innerText = d; pDivSelect.appendChild(opt); }); }
                
                document.getElementById('seasonSelect')?.addEventListener('change', () => loadStats(window.currentProfileName)); 
                document.getElementById('profileDivisionSelect')?.addEventListener('change', () => loadStats(window.currentProfileName));
                
                const boardDivSelect = document.getElementById('boardDiv'); const boardSeasonSelect = document.getElementById('boardSeason');
                if(boardDivSelect) { boardDivSelect.innerHTML = ''; divisions.forEach(d => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = d; opt.innerText = d; boardDivSelect.appendChild(opt); }); }
                if(boardSeasonSelect) { boardSeasonSelect.innerHTML = ''; seasons.forEach(s => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = s; opt.innerText = s; boardSeasonSelect.appendChild(opt); }); boardSeasonSelect.value = latestSeason; }
                
                const resultSeasonSelect = document.getElementById('resultsSeason'); if(resultSeasonSelect) { resultSeasonSelect.innerHTML = ''; seasons.forEach(s => { let opt = document.createElement('option'); opt.value = s; opt.innerText = s; resultSeasonSelect.appendChild(opt); }); resultSeasonSelect.value = latestSeason; }
                
                loadDivisionLeaderboard(); loadResults(); loadTopDonors(); window.loadNotices();
                
                const initialHash = window.location.hash;
                if (initialHash && initialHash !== '#fixtures') {
                    const overlay = document.getElementById('landing-overlay');
                    if(overlay) { overlay.style.display = 'none'; document.body.style.overflow = 'auto'; }
                    
                    if (initialHash.startsWith('#profile/')) {
                        const pName = decodeURIComponent(initialHash.replace('#profile/', ''));
                        loadStats(pName, false);
                    } else {
                        const tabId = initialHash.replace('#', '');
                        if (['home', 'week', 'sheets', 'search', 'notices', 'community', 'live-center', 'rules'].includes(tabId)) {
                            switchTab(tabId, false);
                        } else {
                            switchTab('home', false);
                        }
                    }
                }
            } catch(e) {
                console.error("Initialization Error", e);
            }
        };

        window.onload = async () => {
            generateStars();
            const clientSecret = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('payment_intent_client_secret');
            const paymentIntent = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search).get('payment_intent');
            
            if (clientSecret && paymentIntent) {
                const dName = localStorage.getItem('pending_donation_name') || 'Anonymous'; const dAmt = localStorage.getItem('pending_donation_amount') || 0;
                fetch('/api/record_donation', { method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({intent_id: paymentIntent, name: dName, amount: dAmt}) }).then(() => {
                    localStorage.removeItem('pending_donation_name'); localStorage.removeItem('pending_donation_amount');
                    alert(`Thank you ${dName} for your support! Payment successful. You are on the Honour Board!`);
                    window.history.replaceState({}, document.title, window.location.pathname); enterFixturesMode();
                });
            }
            
            originalLoadInitialData();
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

==> ./frontend/templates/live_matches.html <==
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="en">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>GCTTA - Live Centre</title>
    <style>
        /* BASIC STYLES */
        body { font-family: -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif; background: #f4f4f9; margin: 0; padding: 20px; }
        .container { max-width: 800px; margin: 0 auto; }
        
        /* HEADER & PULSE */
        .live-header { display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: space-between; margin-bottom: 30px; }
        .status-badge { padding: 8px 16px; border-radius: 20px; font-weight: bold; color: white; background: #ccc; }
        .status-badge.active { background: #ff3b30; animation: pulse 1.5s infinite; }
        
        @keyframes pulse {
            0% { box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(255, 59, 48, 0.7); }
            70% { box-shadow: 0 0 0 10px rgba(255, 59, 48, 0); }
            100% { box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(255, 59, 48, 0); }
        }

        /* MATCH CARDS */
        .section-title { font-size: 1.2rem; color: #666; margin-bottom: 15px; border-bottom: 2px solid #ddd; padding-bottom: 5px; }
        .match-card { background: white; border-radius: 12px; padding: 20px; margin-bottom: 15px; box-shadow: 0 2px 5px rgba(0,0,0,0.05); display: flex; justify-content: space-between; align-items: center; cursor: pointer; transition: transform 0.2s; }
        .match-card:hover { transform: translateY(-2px); box-shadow: 0 5px 15px rgba(0,0,0,0.1); }
        
        .table-num { font-size: 0.9rem; font-weight: 800; color: #007aff; text-transform: uppercase; }
        .scores { display: flex; align-items: center; gap: 20px; font-size: 1.5rem; font-weight: bold; }
        .player-name { font-size: 1.1rem; }
        .vs { color: #999; font-size: 0.9rem; margin: 0 10px; }
        .live-indicator { color: #ff3b30; font-size: 0.8rem; font-weight: bold; display: none; }
        .is-live .live-indicator { display: block; }
        
        /* EMPTY STATE */
        .no-matches { text-align: center; color: #999; padding: 40px; }
    </style>
</head>
<body>

<div class="container">
    <div class="live-header">
        <h1>Match Centre</h1>
        <div id="mainStatusBadge" class="status-badge">OFFLINE</div>
    </div>

    <div id="liveSection" style="display:none;">
        <div class="section-title">🔴 LIVE NOW</div>
        <div id="liveContainer"></div>
    </div>

    <div class="section-title">📅 SCHEDULED TODAY</div>
    <div id="scheduledContainer">
        <div class="no-matches">Loading fixtures...</div>
    </div>
</div>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js";
    import { getFirestore, collection, query, where, onSnapshot } 
    from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js";

    // 1. PASTE YOUR CONFIG HERE
    const firebaseConfig = {
        // ... COPY FROM FIREBASE CONSOLE ...
        projectId: "gctta-stats-live" // Based on your previous checks
    };

    const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
    const db = getFirestore(app);

    // 2. GET TODAY'S DATE (dd/MM/yyyy)
    const today = new Date();
    const dateString = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0') + '/' + String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0') + '/' + today.getFullYear();

    console.log("Listening for matches on:", dateString);

    // 3. LISTEN TO DATABASE
    const q = query(collection(db, "fixtures"), where("date", "==", dateString));

    onSnapshot(q, (snapshot) => {
        const liveContainer = document.getElementById("liveContainer");
        const scheduledContainer = document.getElementById("scheduledContainer");
        const liveSection = document.getElementById("liveSection");
        const badge = document.getElementById("mainStatusBadge");

        liveContainer.innerHTML = "";
        scheduledContainer.innerHTML = "";

        let liveCount = 0;

        if (snapshot.empty) {
            scheduledContainer.innerHTML = "<div class='no-matches'>No matches scheduled for today.</div>";
            return;
        }

        snapshot.forEach((doc) => {
            const m = doc.data();
            const isLive = m.live_home_score !== undefined || m.current_server !== undefined;
            
            // HTML Template for a Card
            const cardHTML = `
                <div class="match-card ${isLive ? 'is-live' : ''}" onclick="window.location.href='match_detail.html?id=${doc.id}'">
                    <div>
                        <div class="table-num">Table ${m.table} • ${m.division}</div>
                        <div class="scores">
                            <div class="team">
                                <div class="player-name">${m.home_team}</div>
                            </div>
                            ${isLive ? `<span>${m.live_home_score} - ${m.live_away_score}</span>` : `<span class="vs">vs</span>`}
                            <div class="team">
                                <div class="player-name">${m.away_team}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    ${isLive ? `<div class="live-indicator">● LIVE</div>` : ``}
                </div>
            `;

            if (isLive) {
                liveContainer.innerHTML += cardHTML;
                liveCount++;
            } else {
                scheduledContainer.innerHTML += cardHTML;
            }
        });

        // Toggle "Live Mode"
        if (liveCount > 0) {
            liveSection.style.display = "block";
            badge.textContent = `${liveCount} LIVE`;
            badge.classList.add("active");
        } else {
            liveSection.style.display = "none";
            badge.textContent = "SCHEDULED";
            badge.classList.remove("active");
        }
    });
</script>

</body>
</html>

                <i class="fa-solid fa-user-plus"></i>
            </div>
            <h1 class="text-2xl font-black">Player Registration</h1>
            <p class="text-sm text-slate-400 mt-2">Create your official club account to track stats, register for events, and join the community hub.</p>
        </div>

        <div class="space-y-4">
            <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                <div>
                    <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">First Name</label>
                    <input type="text" id="reg-first" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition-colors">
                </div>
                <div>
                    <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">Last Name</label>
                    <input type="text" id="reg-last" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition-colors">
                </div>
            </div>
            
            <div>
                <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">Date of Birth</label>
                <input type="date" id="reg-dob" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 text-sm transition-colors cursor-pointer">
            </div>
            
            <div>
                <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">Current Rating (Or RC ID)</label>
                <input type="text" id="reg-rating" placeholder="e.g. 1200 or ID: 123456" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition-colors">
            </div>

            <div class="pt-4 border-t border-white/5 mt-2">
                <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">Email Address</label>
                <input type="email" id="reg-email" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 mb-4 transition-colors">
                
                <label class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1 block">Password</label>
                <input type="password" id="reg-password" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition-colors">
            </div>

            <button onclick="registerPlayer()" id="reg-btn" class="w-full bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold py-3.5 rounded-xl mt-6 transition-all shadow-lg hover:shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(79,70,229,0.4)]">Create Account</button>
            
            <p class="text-center text-xs text-slate-500 mt-4">Already have an account? <a href="/login" class="text-indigo-400 hover:text-indigo-300 font-bold transition-colors">Sign in</a></p>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        window.registerPlayer = async function() {
            const first = document.getElementById('reg-first').value.trim();
            const last = document.getElementById('reg-last').value.trim();
            const dob = document.getElementById('reg-dob').value;
            const rating = document.getElementById('reg-rating').value;
            const email = document.getElementById('reg-email').value.trim();
            const pass = document.getElementById('reg-password').value;

            if(!first || !last || !dob || !email || !pass) return alert("Please fill in all required fields.");

            const btn = document.getElementById('reg-btn');
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Creating...';
            btn.disabled = true;

            try {
                // In production, this generates a real Firebase UID. For now we generate a secure mock one.
                const mockUid = 'usr_' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9);
                const fullName = `${first} ${last}`;

                const res = await fetch('/api/hub/register', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
                    body: JSON.stringify({ uid: mockUid, name: fullName, dob: dob, email: email, estimated_rating: rating })
                });
                
                const data = await res.json();
                if(data.success) {
                    localStorage.setItem('player_uid', mockUid);
                    localStorage.setItem('player_name', fullName);
                    window.location.href = '/dashboard';
                } else {
                    alert("Account created, but failed to link to database.");
                }
            } catch(e) {
                alert("Network Error");
            } finally {
                btn.innerHTML = 'Create Account';
                btn.disabled = false;
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        <button id="googleSignInBtn" disabled class="w-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 border border-white/5 font-bold py-3 px-4 rounded-xl transition flex items-center justify-center gap-3 shadow-lg cursor-wait">

            Checking session...
        </button>

        <div id="error-msg" class="hidden mt-4 text-red-400 text-sm font-bold bg-red-900/30 border border-red-500/20 py-2 px-3 rounded-lg"></div>
    </div>

    <script type="module">
        import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js";
        import { getAuth, GoogleAuthProvider, signInWithPopup, onAuthStateChanged, signOut } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-auth.js";

        const firebaseConfig = { apiKey: "AIzaSyDq05wFsKLHtt8G0Z5yLOG9pIk9UX24S4o", authDomain: "gctta-stats-live.firebaseapp.com", projectId: "gctta-stats-live", storageBucket: "gctta-stats-live.firebasestorage.app", messagingSenderId: "1070856258556", appId: "1:1070856258556:web:be438e04c1941abc3c6879" };
        const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
        const auth = getAuth(app);
        const provider = new GoogleAuthProvider();

        const btn = document.getElementById('googleSignInBtn');
        const errorMsg = document.getElementById('error-msg');

        // Helper functions to instantly switch the button's look
        function setButtonActive() {
            btn.disabled = false;
            btn.className = "w-full bg-white hover:bg-slate-100 text-slate-900 font-bold py-3 px-4 rounded-xl transition flex items-center justify-center gap-3 shadow-lg cursor-pointer";
            btn.innerHTML = '<img src="https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/ui/2.0.0/images/auth/google.svg" class="w-5 h-5"> Sign in with Google';
        }

        function setButtonLoading(text) {
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.className = "w-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 border border-white/5 font-bold py-3 px-4 rounded-xl transition flex items-center justify-center gap-3 shadow-lg cursor-wait";
            btn.innerHTML = `<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-lg"></i> ${text}`;
        }

        // --- AUTOMATICALLY RECONNECT EXISTING SESSIONS ---
        onAuthStateChanged(auth, (user) => {
            if (user) {
                setButtonLoading("Restoring Session...");
                
                user.getIdToken(true).then((token) => {
                    return fetch('/api/auth/google', {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
                        body: JSON.stringify({token: token})
                    });
                }).then(res => res.json()).then(data => {
                    if(data.success) { window.location.href = '/admin'; } 
                    else {
                        errorMsg.innerText = data.error;
                        errorMsg.classList.remove('hidden');
                        setButtonActive();
                        signOut(auth); // Kick them out if not an approved admin
                    }
                }).catch(e => {
                    setButtonActive();
                });
            } else {
                // If Firebase confirms NO user is logged in, unlock the button!
                setButtonActive();
            }
        });

        // --- MANUAL LOGIN BUTTON TRIGGER ---
        btn.addEventListener('click', () => {
            setButtonLoading("Authenticating...");
            errorMsg.classList.add('hidden');
            
            signInWithPopup(auth, provider).then((result) => {
                // If successful, onAuthStateChanged (above) will instantly catch it and handle the redirect!
            }).catch(error => {
                errorMsg.innerText = "Popup blocked or login failed.";
                errorMsg.classList.remove('hidden');
                setButtonActive();
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

    <script>
        function toggleAuth(mode) {
            const isLog = mode === 'login';
            document.getElementById('form-login').classList.toggle('hidden', !isLog);
            document.getElementById('form-register').classList.toggle('hidden', isLog);
            
            document.getElementById('btn-login-tab').className = isLog ? "px-6 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow transition-all" : "px-6 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-all";
            document.getElementById('btn-register-tab').className = !isLog ? "px-6 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold bg-indigo-600 text-white shadow transition-all" : "px-6 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-white transition-all";
            
            document.getElementById('auth-title').innerText = isLog ? "Welcome Back" : "Join the Club";
            document.getElementById('auth-subtitle').innerText = isLog ? "Sign in to access your stats and the community hub." : "Create your official player profile.";
        }

        window.loginPlayer = function() {
            const email = document.getElementById('log-email').value;
            if(!email) return alert("Enter email.");
            
            const mockName = email.split('@')[0].replace('.', ' ');
            localStorage.setItem('player_uid', 'usr_' + Date.now());
            localStorage.setItem('player_name', mockName.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + mockName.slice(1));
            window.location.href = '/dashboard';
        };

        window.registerPlayer = async function() {
            const first = document.getElementById('reg-first').value.trim();
            const last = document.getElementById('reg-last').value.trim();
            const dob = document.getElementById('reg-dob').value;
            const rating = document.getElementById('reg-rating').value;
            const email = document.getElementById('reg-email').value.trim();
            const pass = document.getElementById('reg-password').value;

            if(!first || !last || !email || !pass) return alert("Please fill required fields.");

            const btn = document.getElementById('reg-submit-btn');
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Processing...';
            btn.disabled = true;

            const fullName = `${first} ${last}`;
            const mockUid = 'usr_' + Date.now();

            try {
                await fetch('/api/hub/register', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
                    body: JSON.stringify({ uid: mockUid, name: fullName, dob: dob, email: email, estimated_rating: rating })
                });
                
                localStorage.setItem('player_uid', mockUid);
                localStorage.setItem('player_name', fullName);
                window.location.href = '/dashboard';
            } catch(e) {
                alert("Network Error");
                btn.innerHTML = 'Create Account';
                btn.disabled = false;
            }
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

                    <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-sky-400 mb-2 tracking-widest"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-bar mr-1"></i> Create a Poll</div>
                    <input type="text" placeholder="Option 1" class="poll-opt w-full bg-slate-800 text-sm p-2.5 rounded border border-white/10 outline-none focus:border-sky-500 text-white">
                    <input type="text" placeholder="Option 2" class="poll-opt w-full bg-slate-800 text-sm p-2.5 rounded border border-white/10 outline-none focus:border-sky-500 text-white">
                </div>

                <div class="flex justify-between items-center mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-white/5">
                    <div class="flex gap-4">
                        <button onclick="document.getElementById('poll-builder').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="text-sky-400 hover:text-sky-300 text-sm font-bold flex items-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-pie mr-1.5"></i> Poll</button>

            <div class="text-center py-10 text-slate-500 italic">No events currently open for registration.</div>
        </div>
    </div>

    <script>
        const PLAYER_UID = localStorage.getItem('player_uid');
        const PLAYER_NAME = localStorage.getItem('player_name');
        
        if(!PLAYER_UID) window.location.href = '/player_auth';
        document.getElementById('nav-player-name').innerText = PLAYER_NAME;

        function logout() { localStorage.removeItem('player_uid'); localStorage.removeItem('player_name'); window.location.href = '/'; }

        function switchTab(tabId) {
            ['profile', 'forum', 'tournaments'].forEach(t => {
                document.getElementById(`tab-${t}`).classList.add('hidden');
                document.getElementById(`nav-${t}`).classList.remove('text-indigo-400');
                document.getElementById(`nav-${t}`).classList.add('text-slate-500');
            });
            document.getElementById(`tab-${tabId}`).classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById(`nav-${tabId}`).classList.remove('text-slate-500');
            document.getElementById(`nav-${tabId}`).classList.add('text-indigo-400');

            if(tabId === 'profile') loadProfileStats();
            if(tabId === 'forum') loadForum();
        }

        async function loadProfileStats() {
            const container = document.getElementById('hub-stats-container');
            const scheduleList = document.getElementById('hub-schedule-list');
            try {
                const res = await fetch(`/api/stats/${encodeURIComponent(PLAYER_NAME)}`);
                if(res.ok) {
                    const stats = await res.json();
                    container.innerHTML = `
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 md:gap-6 w-full">
                        <div class="bg-indigo-900/20 p-5 rounded-xl border border-indigo-500/30 text-center relative overflow-hidden">
                            <div class="absolute top-0 left-0 w-full h-1 bg-indigo-500"></div>
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-indigo-400 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-1">Glicko Rating</div>
                            <div class="text-4xl font-black text-white font-mono">${stats.rating}</div>
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-mono mt-1 bg-black/30 px-2 py-1 rounded inline-block" title="Rating Deviation (System Confidence)">Standard Dev: ±${stats.rd}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-white/5 text-center flex flex-col justify-center">
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-1">Win Rate</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-black text-emerald-400 font-mono">${stats.combined.win_rate}</div>
                            <div class="text-xs text-slate-400 mt-1">${stats.combined.matches} Matches Played</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                } else {
                    container.innerHTML = `<div class="bg-slate-800 p-6 rounded-xl text-center border border-red-500/20"><p class="text-red-400 font-bold text-sm">No match history found for "${PLAYER_NAME}".</p><p class="text-xs text-slate-500 mt-2">If your name is misspelled in the database, contact an admin to merge your profile.</p></div>`;
                }

                const schedRes = await fetch(`/api/hub/schedule/${encodeURIComponent(PLAYER_NAME)}`);
                if (schedRes.ok) {
                    const matches = await schedRes.json();
                    if (matches.length > 0) {
                        scheduleList.innerHTML = matches.map(m => `
                            <div class="bg-slate-900/50 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shadow-sm">
                                <div class="text-[10px] text-sky-400 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-2 border-b border-white/5 pb-2">${m.division} • ${m.date_text}</div>
                                <div class="text-white font-bold text-sm">${m.home_team} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-xs">VS</span> ${m.away_team}</div>
                                <div class="flex justify-between items-start text-[10px] font-bold text-slate-400 mt-2">
                                    <div class="w-[45%] text-right flex flex-col gap-0.5">${m.home_players ? m.home_players.map(p => `<span>${p}</span>`).join('') : ''}</div>
                                    <div class="w-[10%]"></div>
                                    <div class="w-[45%] text-left flex flex-col gap-0.5">${m.away_players ? m.away_players.map(p => `<span>${p}</span>`).join('') : ''}</div>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        `).join('');
                    } else { scheduleList.innerHTML = `<div class="text-slate-500 text-sm italic py-2">No upcoming matches scheduled.</div>`; }
                }
            } catch(e) {}
        }

        let base64Image = null;
        function previewImage(event) {
            const file = event.target.files[0];
            if(!file) return;
            const reader = new FileReader();
            reader.onload = function(e) { base64Image = e.target.result; document.getElementById('image-preview').src = base64Image; document.getElementById('image-preview-container').classList.remove('hidden'); };
            reader.readAsDataURL(file);
        }
        function removeImage() { base64Image = null; document.getElementById('image-preview-container').classList.add('hidden'); }

        async function submitForumPost() {
            const val = document.getElementById('forum-input').value.trim();
            const pollOpts = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.poll-opt')).map(i => i.value.trim()).filter(v => v);
            if(!val && !base64Image && pollOpts.length === 0) return;

            const btn = document.getElementById('btn-post'); btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>'; btn.disabled = true;
            try {
                await fetch('/api/hub/post', { 
                    method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ uid: PLAYER_UID, name: PLAYER_NAME, content: val, type: pollOpts.length > 0 ? 'Poll' : 'General', image_url: base64Image, poll_options: pollOpts.length > 0 ? pollOpts : null }) 
                });
                document.getElementById('forum-input').value = ''; removeImage();
                document.querySelectorAll('.poll-opt').forEach(i => i.value = ''); document.getElementById('poll-builder').classList.add('hidden');
                loadForum();
            } catch(e) {} finally { btn.innerHTML = 'Post'; btn.disabled = false; }
        }

        async function loadForum() {
            const feed = document.getElementById('forum-feed');
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/hub/forum'); const posts = await res.json();
                if(posts.length === 0) { feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-500 italic py-10">Start the conversation!</div>'; return; }
                
                feed.innerHTML = posts.map(p => {
                    const imgHtml = p.image_url ? `<img src="${p.image_url}" class="mt-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 max-h-80 w-full object-cover shadow-lg">` : '';
                    let pollHtml = '';
                    if (p.type === 'Poll' && p.poll) {
                        let totalVotes = 0; for(const voters of Object.values(p.poll)) totalVotes += voters.length;
                        pollHtml = `<div class="mt-4 space-y-2">`;
                        for(const [opt, voters] of Object.entries(p.poll)) {
                            const pct = totalVotes > 0 ? Math.round((voters.length / totalVotes) * 100) : 0;
                            const hasVoted = voters.includes(PLAYER_UID);
                            const activeClass = hasVoted ? "border-sky-500 text-sky-400" : "border-white/10 hover:border-white/30 text-white";
                            const barColor = hasVoted ? "bg-sky-600/30" : "bg-slate-700/50";
                            
                            pollHtml += `
                            <div onclick="votePoll('${p.id}', '${opt.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="relative overflow-hidden border rounded-lg p-3 cursor-pointer transition-all ${activeClass} bg-black/40">
                                <div class="absolute top-0 left-0 h-full ${barColor} transition-all duration-500" style="width: ${pct}%"></div>
                                <div class="relative flex justify-between items-center text-sm font-bold z-10"><span>${opt}</span><span>${pct}%</span></div>
                            </div>`;
                        }
                        pollHtml += `<div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 text-right mt-1 font-mono">${totalVotes} votes</div></div>`;
                    }

                    const upvotes = p.upvotes || []; const isLiked = upvotes.includes(PLAYER_UID);
                    const comments = p.comments || [];
                    let commentsHtml = comments.length > 0 ? `<div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/5 space-y-3">` + comments.map(c => `<div class="bg-slate-900/50 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5"><div class="text-[10px] text-indigo-400 font-bold mb-1">${c.author}</div><div class="text-xs text-slate-300">${c.content}</div></div>`).join('') + `</div>` : '';

                    return `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 md:p-6 rounded-2xl border border-white/5 shadow-xl">
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                                <div class="w-10 h-10 bg-gradient-to-br from-indigo-600 to-purple-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center font-black text-white shadow-lg">${p.author_name.charAt(0)}</div>
                                <div><div class="text-sm font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-1">${p.author_name} <i class="fa-solid fa-circle-check text-sky-400 text-[10px]" title="Verified Profile"></i></div><div class="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-mono">${p.time_str}</div></div>
                            </div>
                            ${p.type === 'Poll' ? '<span class="bg-sky-900/30 text-sky-400 border border-sky-500/30 text-[9px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded shadow uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">Poll</span>' : ''}
                        </div>
                        <p class="text-sm text-slate-200 whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed">${p.content}</p>
                        ${imgHtml}
                        ${pollHtml}
                        <div class="mt-5 flex items-center gap-6">
                            <button onclick="toggleLike('${p.id}')" class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold transition-transform hover:scale-110 ${isLiked ? 'text-pink-500' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-pink-400'}"><i class="fa-solid fa-heart"></i> ${upvotes.length}</button>
                            <button onclick="document.getElementById('comment-box-${p.id}').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors"><i class="fa-solid fa-comment"></i> ${comments.length}</button>
                        </div>
                        ${commentsHtml}
                        <div id="comment-box-${p.id}" class="hidden mt-4 flex gap-2">
                            <input type="text" id="comment-input-${p.id}" placeholder="Write a reply..." class="flex-1 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-xs text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500">
                            <button onclick="submitComment('${p.id}')" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold px-5 rounded-lg text-xs transition shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i></button>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }).join('');
            } catch(e) {}
        }
        
        async function votePoll(postId, option) { await fetch('/api/hub/vote', { method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, option: option, uid: PLAYER_UID }) }); loadForum(); }
        async function toggleLike(postId) { await fetch('/api/hub/upvote', { method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, uid: PLAYER_UID }) }); loadForum(); }
        async function submitComment(postId) {
            const input = document.getElementById(`comment-input-${postId}`); if(!input.value.trim()) return;
            await fetch('/api/hub/comment', { method: 'POST', headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, name: PLAYER_NAME, content: input.value.trim() }) }); loadForum();
        }
        
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => { switchTab('profile'); });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

<div id="tab-community" class="hidden w-full max-w-3xl mx-auto px-4 pt-6 pb-24 animate-fade-in relative z-10">
    <div class="text-center mb-8">
        <h2 class="text-3xl font-black text-white tracking-tight">Community Hub</h2>
        <p class="text-sm text-slate-400 mt-2">Banter, lost & found, gear questions, and polls.</p>
    </div>

    <div class="bg-slate-800/80 backdrop-blur-xl p-5 rounded-2xl border border-white/10 mb-8 shadow-xl">
        <div id="auth-prompt" class="text-center py-4">
            <p class="text-slate-300 text-sm mb-4">You must be signed in to post, vote, and comment.</p>
            <a href="/player_auth" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold py-2.5 px-6 rounded-lg text-sm transition shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(79,70,229,0.4)]">Sign In / Register</a>
        </div>

        <div id="post-creator" class="hidden">
            <textarea id="pub-forum-input" placeholder="Start a discussion..." class="w-full bg-slate-900/50 border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-4 text-white text-sm resize-none outline-none focus:border-indigo-500 transition-colors" rows="3"></textarea>
            
            <div id="pub-image-preview-container" class="hidden mt-3 relative inline-block">
                <img id="pub-image-preview" src="" class="h-32 rounded-lg border border-white/10 object-cover shadow-lg">
                <button onclick="pubRemoveImage()" class="absolute -top-2 -right-2 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-full w-6 h-6 flex items-center justify-center text-xs shadow hover:scale-110 transition"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark"></i></button>
            </div>

            <div id="pub-poll-builder" class="hidden mt-3 p-4 bg-slate-900 rounded-xl border border-sky-500/30 space-y-2 relative">
                <button onclick="document.getElementById('pub-poll-builder').classList.add('hidden')" class="absolute top-2 right-2 text-slate-500 hover:text-red-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-xmark"></i></button>
                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-sky-400 mb-2 tracking-widest"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-bar mr-1"></i> Create a Poll</div>
                <input type="text" placeholder="Option 1" class="pub-poll-opt w-full bg-slate-800 text-sm p-2.5 rounded border border-white/10 outline-none focus:border-sky-500 text-white">
                <input type="text" placeholder="Option 2" class="pub-poll-opt w-full bg-slate-800 text-sm p-2.5 rounded border border-white/10 outline-none focus:border-sky-500 text-white">

                    <button onclick="document.getElementById('pub-poll-builder').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="text-sky-400 hover:text-sky-300 text-sm font-bold flex items-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-pie mr-1.5"></i> Poll</button>

                        <input type="file" accept="image/*" class="hidden" onchange="pubPreviewImage(event)">
                    </label>

<script>
    let pubBase64Image = null;
    const authHeaders = () => ({
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        'Authorization': 'Bearer ' + (localStorage.getItem('player_token') || '')
    });

    function pubPreviewImage(event) {
        const file = event.target.files[0];
        if(!file) return;
        const reader = new FileReader();
        reader.onload = function(e) { pubBase64Image = e.target.result; document.getElementById('pub-image-preview').src = pubBase64Image; document.getElementById('pub-image-preview-container').classList.remove('hidden'); };
        reader.readAsDataURL(file);
    }
    
    function pubRemoveImage() { pubBase64Image = null; document.getElementById('pub-image-preview-container').classList.add('hidden'); }

    window.initCommunity = function() {
        const uid = localStorage.getItem('player_uid');
        if(!uid) {
            document.getElementById('auth-prompt').classList.remove('hidden');
            document.getElementById('post-creator').classList.add('hidden');
        } else {
            document.getElementById('auth-prompt').classList.add('hidden');
            document.getElementById('post-creator').classList.remove('hidden');
        }
        pubLoadForum();
    };

    async function pubSubmitPost() {
        const val = document.getElementById('pub-forum-input').value.trim();
        const pollOpts = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.pub-poll-opt')).map(i => i.value.trim()).filter(v => v);
        if(!val && !pubBase64Image && pollOpts.length === 0) return;

        const btn = document.getElementById('pub-btn-post'); btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>'; btn.disabled = true;
        try {
            await fetch('/api/hub/post', { 
                method: 'POST', headers: authHeaders(), 
                body: JSON.stringify({ 
                    uid: localStorage.getItem('player_uid'), 
                    name: localStorage.getItem('player_name'), 
                    content: val, 
                    type: pollOpts.length > 0 ? 'Poll' : 'General', 
                    image_url: pubBase64Image, 
                    poll_options: pollOpts.length > 0 ? pollOpts : null 
                }) 
            });
            document.getElementById('pub-forum-input').value = ''; pubRemoveImage();
            document.querySelectorAll('.pub-poll-opt').forEach(i => i.value = ''); document.getElementById('pub-poll-builder').classList.add('hidden');
            pubLoadForum();
        } catch(e) {} finally { btn.innerHTML = 'Post'; btn.disabled = false; }
    }

    async function pubLoadForum() {
        const feed = document.getElementById('pub-forum-feed');
        const uid = localStorage.getItem('player_uid');
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/hub/forum'); const posts = await res.json();
            if(posts.length === 0) { feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-500 italic py-10 bg-slate-800/50 rounded-2xl border border-white/5">Start the conversation!</div>'; return; }
            
            feed.innerHTML = posts.map(p => {
                const imgHtml = p.image_url ? `<img src="${p.image_url}" class="mt-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 max-h-80 w-full object-cover shadow-lg">` : '';
                let pollHtml = '';
                if (p.type === 'Poll' && p.poll) {
                    let totalVotes = 0; for(const voters of Object.values(p.poll)) totalVotes += voters.length;
                    pollHtml = `<div class="mt-4 space-y-2">`;
                    for(const [opt, voters] of Object.entries(p.poll)) {
                        const pct = totalVotes > 0 ? Math.round((voters.length / totalVotes) * 100) : 0;
                        const hasVoted = uid ? voters.includes(uid) : false;
                        const activeClass = hasVoted ? "border-sky-500 text-sky-400" : "border-white/10 hover:border-white/30 text-white";
                        const barColor = hasVoted ? "bg-sky-600/30" : "bg-slate-700/50";
                        
                        pollHtml += `
                        <div ${uid ? `onclick="pubVotePoll('${p.id}', '${opt.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')"` : `onclick="alert('Please sign in to vote.')"`} class="relative overflow-hidden border rounded-lg p-3 cursor-pointer transition-all ${activeClass} bg-black/40">
                            <div class="absolute top-0 left-0 h-full ${barColor} transition-all duration-500" style="width: ${pct}%"></div>
                            <div class="relative flex justify-between items-center text-sm font-bold z-10"><span>${opt}</span><span>${pct}%</span></div>
                        </div>`;
                    }
                    pollHtml += `<div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 text-right mt-1 font-mono">${totalVotes} votes</div></div>`;
                }

                const upvotes = p.upvotes || []; const isLiked = uid ? upvotes.includes(uid) : false;
                const comments = p.comments || [];
                let commentsHtml = comments.length > 0 ? `<div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/5 space-y-3">` + comments.map(c => `<div class="bg-slate-900/50 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5"><div class="text-[10px] text-indigo-400 font-bold mb-1">${c.author}</div><div class="text-xs text-slate-300">${c.content}</div></div>`).join('') + `</div>` : '';

                return `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 md:p-6 rounded-2xl border border-white/5 shadow-xl">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                            <div class="w-10 h-10 bg-gradient-to-br from-indigo-600 to-purple-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center font-black text-white shadow-lg">${p.author_name.charAt(0)}</div>
                            <div><div class="text-sm font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-1">${p.author_name} <i class="fa-solid fa-circle-check text-sky-400 text-[10px]" title="Verified Profile"></i></div><div class="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-mono">${p.time_str}</div></div>
                        </div>
                        ${p.type === 'Poll' ? '<span class="bg-sky-900/30 text-sky-400 border border-sky-500/30 text-[9px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded shadow uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">Poll</span>' : ''}
                    </div>
                    <p class="text-sm text-slate-200 whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed">${p.content}</p>
                    ${imgHtml}
                    ${pollHtml}
                    <div class="mt-5 flex items-center gap-6">
                        <button ${uid ? `onclick="pubToggleLike('${p.id}')"` : `onclick="alert('Please sign in to like.')"`} class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold transition-transform hover:scale-110 ${isLiked ? 'text-pink-500' : 'text-slate-400 hover:text-pink-400'}"><i class="fa-solid fa-heart"></i> ${upvotes.length}</button>
                        <button onclick="document.getElementById('pub-comment-box-${p.id}').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-indigo-400 transition-colors"><i class="fa-solid fa-comment"></i> ${comments.length}</button>
                    </div>
                    ${commentsHtml}
                    <div id="pub-comment-box-${p.id}" class="hidden mt-4 flex gap-2">
                        <input type="text" id="pub-comment-input-${p.id}" placeholder="Write a reply..." class="flex-1 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-4 py-2.5 text-xs text-white outline-none focus:border-indigo-500">
                        <button ${uid ? `onclick="pubSubmitComment('${p.id}')"` : `onclick="alert('Please sign in to comment.')"`} class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold px-5 rounded-lg text-xs transition shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-paper-plane"></i></button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch(e) {}
    }
    
    async function pubVotePoll(postId, option) { await fetch('/api/hub/vote', { method: 'POST', headers: authHeaders(), body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, option: option, uid: localStorage.getItem('player_uid') }) }); pubLoadForum(); }
    async function pubToggleLike(postId) { await fetch('/api/hub/upvote', { method: 'POST', headers: authHeaders(), body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, uid: localStorage.getItem('player_uid') }) }); pubLoadForum(); }
    async function pubSubmitComment(postId) {
        const input = document.getElementById(`pub-comment-input-${postId}`); if(!input.value.trim()) return;
        await fetch('/api/hub/comment', { method: 'POST', headers: authHeaders(), body: JSON.stringify({ post_id: postId, name: localStorage.getItem('player_name'), content: input.value.trim() }) }); pubLoadForum();
    }
</script>
==> ./frontend/templates/Components/home.html <==
<div id="tab-home" class="w-full max-w-6xl px-4 animate-fade-in block relative z-10 mx-auto mt-6 md:mt-12 mb-20">
    <div class="text-center mb-8 relative">
        <div class="inline-block relative">
            <div class="absolute inset-0 bg-yellow-500 blur-3xl opacity-20 rounded-full"></div>
            <img src="https://img.icons8.com/color/144/table-tennis.png" alt="Icon" class="w-24 h-24 md:w-32 md:h-32 relative z-10 drop-shadow-2xl opacity-90 hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-500">
        </div>
        <h2 class="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-black text-white mb-4 tracking-tight drop-shadow-lg mt-6">GCTTA STATS</h2>

            </div>
