==> ./frontend/templates/Components/scripts.html <==
<script>
    // ==========================================
    // MAIN SEARCH LOGIC 
    // ==========================================
    window.allPlayersRaw = []; 

    window.setupMainSearch = function() {
        const topNavSearch = document.getElementById('playerSearch');
        const bigSearch = document.getElementById('bigPlayerSearch');
        
        if (topNavSearch) bindSearchLogic(topNavSearch, 'suggestions-list');
        if (bigSearch) bindSearchLogic(bigSearch, 'big-suggestions-list');
    };

    function bindSearchLogic(inputElement, suggestionsContainerId) {
        const suggContainer = document.getElementById(suggestionsContainerId);
        if (!suggContainer) return;

        inputElement.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const query = e.target.value.toLowerCase().trim();
            
            if (query.length < 2) {
                suggContainer.classList.add('hidden');
                return;
            }

            const matches = window.allPlayersRaw.filter(p => p.toLowerCase().includes(query));
            
            if (matches.length === 0) {
                suggContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="p-4 text-center text-slate-500 italic text-sm">No players found.</div>';
                suggContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
                return;
            }

            suggContainer.innerHTML = matches.slice(0, 10).map(p => `
                <div onclick="window.loadStats('${p.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="px-4 py-3 hover:bg-sky-900/30 cursor-pointer text-white font-bold border-b border-white/5 transition-colors flex justify-between items-center group">
                    <span class="group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors">${p}</span>
                    <i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right text-slate-600 group-hover:text-sky-500 transition-colors text-xs"></i>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            
            suggContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
        });

        // Hide when clicking outside
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
            if (e.target !== inputElement && e.target !== suggContainer && !suggContainer.contains(e.target)) {
                suggContainer.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        });
    }

    // ==========================================
    // UI ENGINE & NAVIGATION
    // ==========================================
    window.switchTab = function(tabId) {
        const tabs = ['home', 'search', 'standings', 'results', 'profile', 'community', 'live'];
        tabs.forEach(t => {
            const el = document.getElementById(t + 'Container');
            if(el) el.classList.add('hidden');
            
            const navBtn = document.getElementById('nav-' + t);
            if(navBtn) {
                navBtn.classList.remove('text-yellow-400', 'scale-110');
                navBtn.classList.add('text-slate-500');
            }
        });
        
        const targetEl = document.getElementById(tabId + 'Container');
        if(targetEl) targetEl.classList.remove('hidden');
        
        const targetNavBtn = document.getElementById('nav-' + (tabId === 'profile' ? 'search' : tabId));
        if(targetNavBtn) {
            targetNavBtn.classList.remove('text-slate-500');
            targetNavBtn.classList.add('text-yellow-400', 'scale-110');
        }

        if(tabId === 'results') window.loadResultsData();
        if(tabId === 'community') window.loadCommunityFeed();
    };

    window.closeProfile = function() {
        document.getElementById('statsContainer').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('searchContainer').classList.remove('hidden');
    };

    // ==========================================
    // STATS PROFILES & TOGGLE LOGIC
    // ==========================================
    window.currentProfileName = "";
    window.currentProfileData = null;

    window.loadStats = async function(playerName, pushHistory = true) {
        window.currentProfileName = playerName;
        if (pushHistory) { history.pushState({ page: 'profile', name: playerName }, "", "#profile/" + encodeURIComponent(playerName)); }
        
        ['home', 'week', 'sheets', 'search', 'notices', 'community', 'live-center', 'rules'].forEach(t => { 
            const el = document.getElementById(`tab-${t}`); 
            if(el) el.classList.add('hidden'); 
        });
        
        const statsContainer = document.getElementById('statsContainer');
        if (statsContainer) {
            statsContainer.classList.remove('hidden');
            statsContainer.classList.add('animate-fade-in');
        }

        document.getElementById('playerName').innerText = playerName;
        document.getElementById('playerRatingBadge').innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>';
        
        const season = document.getElementById('seasonSelect')?.value || 'Career';
        const division = document.getElementById('profileDivisionSelect')?.value || 'All';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/stats/${encodeURIComponent(playerName)}?season=${encodeURIComponent(season)}&division=${encodeURIComponent(division)}`);
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error("Player not found");
            const d = await res.json();
            window.currentProfileData = d;
            
            window.renderProfile();
            
        } catch(e) {
            document.getElementById('playerRatingBadge').innerHTML = "N/A";
            document.getElementById('matchHistory').innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-red-500">Error loading profile data.</div>';
        }
    };

    window.renderProfile = function() {
        if (!window.currentProfileData) return;
        const d = window.currentProfileData;
        
        // Dynamic Toggle Logic (Visual & Data)
        const toggleEl = document.getElementById('profileFillinToggle');
        const isCombined = toggleEl ? toggleEl.checked : true; 
        
        const toggleBg = document.getElementById('toggleBg');
        const toggleDot = document.getElementById('toggleDot');
        
        if (toggleBg && toggleDot) {
            if (isCombined) {
                toggleBg.classList.remove('bg-slate-600');
                toggleBg.classList.add('bg-sky-500');
                toggleDot.classList.add('translate-x-5');
            } else {
                toggleBg.classList.remove('bg-sky-500');
                toggleBg.classList.add('bg-slate-600');
                toggleDot.classList.remove('translate-x-5');
            }
        }
        
        // If checked, show Combined (Regular + Fill-in). If unchecked, show Regular only.
        const displayStats = isCombined ? d.combined : d.regular; 
        
        document.getElementById('playerRatingBadge').innerHTML = `
            ${d.rating} <span class="text-[10px] text-sky-400 font-bold ml-1">±${d.rd}</span>
        `;
        
        document.getElementById('matchesPlayed').innerText = displayStats.matches || 0;
        document.getElementById('wins').innerText = displayStats.wins || 0;
        document.getElementById('losses').innerText = displayStats.losses || 0;
        document.getElementById('winRate').innerText = displayStats.win_rate || "0%";

        const histContainer = document.getElementById('matchHistory');
        if (!displayStats.match_history || displayStats.match_history.length === 0) {
            histContainer.innerHTML = '<div class="p-10 text-center text-slate-500 italic border border-white/5 rounded-xl bg-slate-800/30 text-sm">No match history available for this filter.</div>';
            return;
        }

        histContainer.innerHTML = displayStats.match_history.map(m => {
            const won = m.result === 'Win';
            const bgColor = won ? 'bg-green-500/10' : 'bg-red-500/10';
            const borderColor = won ? 'border-green-500/20' : 'border-red-500/20';
            const textColor = won ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400';
            const icon = won ? 'fa-check' : 'fa-xmark';
            
            const delta = m.delta || 0;
            const deltaStr = (delta > 0 ? '+' : '') + delta.toFixed(1);
            const deltaColor = delta > 0 ? 'text-emerald-400' : (delta < 0 ? 'text-red-400' : 'text-slate-500');
            const deltaBadge = `<span class="${deltaColor} text-[10px] font-mono font-black ml-2 bg-black/40 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded border border-white/5 shadow-inner">${deltaStr} <i class="fa-solid ${delta > 0 ? 'fa-arrow-trend-up' : (delta < 0 ? 'fa-arrow-trend-down' : 'fa-minus')} ml-1"></i></span>`;
            
            let detailsHtml = m.details ? `<div class="mt-3 text-xs font-mono text-slate-400 bg-black/20 p-2.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5 tracking-wider">${m.details}</div>` : '';
            
            return `
            <div class="p-4 md:p-5 border-b border-white/5 last:border-0 hover:bg-white/5 transition-colors ${bgColor}">
                <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 md:gap-3 flex-wrap">
                        <span class="${textColor} font-black text-sm md:text-base flex items-center"><i class="fa-solid ${icon} mr-1.5 md:mr-2"></i>${m.result}</span>
                        <span class="text-[10px] md:text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono tracking-widest bg-black/40 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border ${borderColor}">${m.date}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center">
                        <span class="font-black text-base md:text-lg ${textColor} font-mono tracking-tighter bg-black/40 px-3 py-0.5 rounded-lg border ${borderColor} shadow-inner">${m.score}</span>
                        ${deltaBadge}
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="text-sm md:text-base text-slate-200"><span class="text-slate-500 text-xs mr-2 uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">vs</span> <span class="font-bold hover:text-sky-400 cursor-pointer transition-colors" onclick="window.loadStats('${m.opponent.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">${m.opponent}</span></div>
                ${detailsHtml}
            </div>`;
        }).join('');
    }

    // ==========================================
    // STANDINGS / LEADERBOARDS
    // ==========================================
    window.loadDivisionLeaderboard = async function() {
        const season = document.getElementById('boardSeason')?.value;
        const division = document.getElementById('boardDiv')?.value;
        const list = document.getElementById('divisionStandingsList');
        
        if (!list || !season || !division) return;
        
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-sky-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-3xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/rankings/${encodeURIComponent(season)}/${encodeURIComponent(division)}`);
            let rankings = await res.json();
            
            rankings = rankings.filter(r => r.regular && r.regular.matches > 0);
            
            rankings.sort((a, b) => {
                const winRateA = a.regular.matches > 0 ? (a.regular.wins / a.regular.matches) : 0;
                const winRateB = b.regular.matches > 0 ? (b.regular.wins / b.regular.matches) : 0;
                if (winRateB !== winRateA) return winRateB - winRateA;
                return b.regular.wins - a.regular.wins;
            });
            
            if (rankings.length === 0) {
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-500 italic mt-8 bg-slate-800/30 p-8 rounded-xl border border-white/5 text-sm">No regular season data available.</div>';
                return;
            }
            
            list.innerHTML = rankings.map((r, index) => {
                const winRate = Math.round((r.regular.wins / r.regular.matches) * 100);
                const isTop3 = index < 3;
                
                let rankBadge = `<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 flex items-center justify-center font-black text-sm border border-white/10 shrink-0 shadow-inner">${index + 1}</div>`;
                if(index === 0) rankBadge = `<div class="w-9 h-9 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-yellow-300 to-yellow-600 text-black flex items-center justify-center font-black text-lg shrink-0 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(250,204,21,0.5)] border border-yellow-200"><i class="fa-solid fa-trophy"></i></div>`;
                if(index === 1) rankBadge = `<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-slate-300 to-slate-500 text-black flex items-center justify-center font-black text-base shrink-0 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(148,163,184,0.4)] border border-slate-200">2</div>`;
                if(index === 2) rankBadge = `<div class="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-gradient-to-br from-orange-400 to-orange-700 text-black flex items-center justify-center font-black text-base shrink-0 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(249,115,22,0.4)] border border-orange-300">3</div>`;
                
                return `
                <div onclick="window.loadStats('${r.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="bg-slate-800/80 p-3 md:p-4 rounded-xl border ${isTop3 ? 'border-sky-500/30' : 'border-white/5'} mb-2 md:mb-3 flex items-center justify-between cursor-pointer hover:bg-slate-700 transition shadow-lg group">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3 md:gap-4 flex-1 min-w-0">
                        ${rankBadge}
                        <div class="min-w-0 pr-3">
                            <div class="font-black text-white text-sm md:text-base group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors truncate">${r.name}</div>
                            <div class="text-[10px] md:text-xs text-slate-500 font-mono mt-0.5 flex items-center gap-2">
                                <span>R: ${r.rating_val} <span class="text-slate-600">±${r.sigma}</span></span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-4 md:gap-6 shrink-0">
                        <div class="text-center hidden sm:block">
                            <div class="text-white font-black text-sm">${r.regular.wins}-${r.regular.losses}</div>
                            <div class="text-[9px] uppercase tracking-widest text-slate-500 font-bold">W-L</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-right w-16">
                            <div class="text-lg md:text-xl font-black ${winRate >= 50 ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'} font-mono">${winRate}%</div>
                        </div>
                        <i class="fa-solid fa-chevron-right text-slate-600 text-xs hidden md:block"></i>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch(e) {
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-red-500 text-sm border border-red-500/20 bg-red-900/10 rounded-xl">Error loading standings.</div>';
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MATCH CENTRE (Results Tab)
    // ==========================================
    window.loadResults = async function() {
        const season = document.getElementById('resultsSeason')?.value;
        const week = document.getElementById('resultsWeek')?.value || '1';
        const list = document.getElementById('resultsList');
        
        if (!list || !season) return;
        
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-sky-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-3xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/week/${encodeURIComponent(season)}/${encodeURIComponent(week)}`);
            const matches = await res.json();
            
            if (matches.length === 0) {
                list.innerHTML = `<div class="text-center text-slate-500 italic mt-8 bg-slate-800/30 p-8 rounded-xl border border-white/5 text-sm">No matches found for Week ${week}.</div>`;
                return;
            }
            
            let html = '';
            matches.forEach(m => {
                let s1 = 0, s2 = 0;
                if (m.score && m.score.includes('-')) {
                    const parts = m.score.split('-');
                    s1 = parseInt(parts[0]) || 0;
                    s2 = parseInt(parts[1]) || 0;
                }
                
                const p1Won = s1 > s2;
                const p2Won = s2 > s1;
                
                html += `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 mb-3 shadow-lg hover:border-white/10 transition-colors">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-3 border-b border-white/5 pb-2">
                        <span class="text-[10px] font-bold uppercase tracking-widest text-sky-400 bg-sky-900/20 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-sky-500/20">${m.division || 'Unknown Div'}</span>
                        <span class="text-[10px] font-mono text-slate-500">${m.date || 'No Date'}</span>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="grid grid-cols-[1fr,auto,1fr] gap-4 items-center">
                        <div class="text-right cursor-pointer group" onclick="window.loadStats('${m.p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                            <div class="text-sm md:text-base font-black ${p1Won ? 'text-white' : 'text-slate-400'} group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors">${m.p1}</div>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="flex items-center justify-center bg-black/40 px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg border border-white/5">
                            <span class="font-mono font-black text-lg ${p1Won ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-white'}">${s1}</span>
                            <span class="text-slate-600 mx-2">-</span>
                            <span class="font-mono font-black text-lg ${p2Won ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-white'}">${s2}</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="text-left cursor-pointer group" onclick="window.loadStats('${m.p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                            <div class="text-sm md:text-base font-black ${p2Won ? 'text-white' : 'text-slate-400'} group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors">${m.p2}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) {
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-red-500 text-sm border border-red-500/20 bg-red-900/10 rounded-xl">Error loading match results.</div>';
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // NOTICES & COMMUNITY
    // ==========================================
    window.loadNotices = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('noticesFeed');
        if(!list) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/notices');
            const notices = await res.json();
            if(notices.length === 0) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic">No recent notices.</div>'; return; }
            
            list.innerHTML = notices.map(n => {
                let colorClass = 'border-slate-500/30 text-slate-300';
                if(n.type === 'Update') colorClass = 'border-sky-500/30 text-sky-400 bg-sky-900/10';
                if(n.type === 'Event') colorClass = 'border-yellow-500/30 text-yellow-400 bg-yellow-900/10';
                if(n.type === 'Alert') colorClass = 'border-red-500/30 text-red-400 bg-red-900/10';
                return `
                <div class="p-5 rounded-xl border ${colorClass} mb-4 shadow-lg">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-3">
                        <h4 class="font-black text-lg leading-tight text-white">${n.title}</h4>
                        <span class="text-[10px] font-mono opacity-70 shrink-0 ml-3 bg-black/40 px-2 py-1 rounded">${n.date_str}</span>
                    </div>
                    <p class="text-sm opacity-90 leading-relaxed whitespace-pre-wrap">${n.message}</p>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.loadCommunityFeed = async function() {
        const feed = document.getElementById('communityFeed');
        if(!feed) return;
        feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-sky-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/hub/forum');
            const posts = await res.json();
            if(posts.length === 0) { feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-500 py-10 italic border border-white/5 rounded-xl bg-slate-800/30 text-sm">No posts yet. Be the first!</div>'; return; }
            
            feed.innerHTML = posts.map(p => `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shadow-xl mb-4 relative">
                    <div class="flex items-center justify-between mb-3 border-b border-white/5 pb-3">
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3 cursor-pointer group" onclick="window.loadStats('${p.author_name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')">
                            <div class="w-10 h-10 rounded-full bg-slate-700 flex items-center justify-center text-slate-400 border border-white/10 shrink-0 group-hover:bg-sky-900/50 group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors"><i class="fa-solid fa-user"></i></div>
                            <div>
                                <div class="font-bold text-white text-sm leading-tight group-hover:text-sky-400 transition-colors">${p.author_name}</div>
                                <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono tracking-widest">${p.time_str}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-sm md:text-base text-slate-200 mb-4 whitespace-pre-wrap leading-relaxed">${p.content}</div>
                    ${p.image_url ? `<img src="${p.image_url}" class="w-full rounded-xl mb-4 max-h-96 object-cover border border-white/10 shadow-lg">` : ''}
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch(e) { feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-500 text-center py-10 text-sm">Failed to load feed.</div>'; }
    };
    
    window.loadTopDonors = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('donorsList');
        if(!list) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/top_donors');
            const donors = await res.json();
            if (donors.length === 0) return;
            
            list.innerHTML = donors.map((d, i) => `
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5 mb-2">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <span class="text-xs font-black ${i===0 ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text-slate-500'}">#${i+1}</span>
                        <span class="text-sm font-bold text-white truncate">${d.name}</span>
                    </div>
                    <span class="text-emerald-400 font-mono font-bold">$${Math.round(d.amount)}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.gcttaData = { players: [], seasons: [], divisions: [], cache: {} };

    window.initApp = async function() {
        try {
            const [playersRes, seasonsRes, divisionsRes] = await Promise.all([
                fetch('/api/players'), fetch('/api/seasons'), fetch('/api/divisions')
            ]);
            window.allPlayersRaw = await playersRes.json();
            window.gcttaData.players = window.allPlayersRaw;
            window.gcttaData.seasons = await seasonsRes.json();
            window.gcttaData.divisions = await divisionsRes.json();
            
            const seasonSelect = document.getElementById('standingSeason');
            const divSelect = document.getElementById('standingDivision');
            if(seasonSelect) seasonSelect.innerHTML = window.gcttaData.seasons.map(s => `<option value="${s}" ${s === window.gcttaData.seasons[0] ? 'selected' : ''}>${s}</option>`).join('');
            if(divSelect) divSelect.innerHTML = window.gcttaData.divisions.map(d => `<option value="${d}" ${d === 'Division 1' ? 'selected' : ''}>${d}</option>`).join('');

            const resultsSeason = document.getElementById('resultsSeason');
            if(resultsSeason) resultsSeason.innerHTML = window.gcttaData.seasons.map(s => `<option value="${s}" ${s === window.gcttaData.seasons[0] ? 'selected' : ''}>${s}</option>`).join('');

        } catch (e) {
            console.error("Initialization Failed", e);
        }
    };
</script>

<div class="space-y-6 animate-fade-in w-full max-w-4xl mx-auto">

                    <option value="All">All Divisions</option>
                </select>
                <input type="text" id="hist-date-filter" placeholder="Filter Date (DD/MM/YYYY)" class="bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-white text-sm rounded-lg px-4 py-3 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none font-mono min-w-[180px]" onkeyup="if(event.key === 'Enter') window.searchHistory()">
                <button onclick="window.searchHistory()" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold px-6 py-3 rounded-lg transition shadow-lg shrink-0">Search</button>
            </div>
        </div>
        
        <div id="historyList" class="space-y-3 max-h-[600px] overflow-y-auto pr-2 custom-scrollbar">
            <div class="text-center py-10 text-slate-500 italic">Enter a search query to pull historical records.</div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

==> ./frontend/templates/Components/Admin/scripts.html <==
<script>
    console.log("✅ Admin UI Script Loaded Successfully!");

    // ==========================================
    // UI NAVIGATION ENGINE
    // ==========================================
    window.setAdminCategory = function(catId) {
        ['ops', 'players', 'setup', 'comms', 'system'].forEach(c => {
            const btn = document.getElementById(`cat-${c}`);
            if (btn) { 
                btn.classList.remove('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-400'); 
                btn.classList.add('border-transparent', 'text-slate-500'); 
            }
            const sub = document.getElementById(`sub-${c}`);
            if (sub) {
                sub.classList.add('hidden');
            }
        });

        const targetBtn = document.getElementById(`cat-${catId}`);
        if (targetBtn) { 
            targetBtn.classList.remove('border-transparent', 'text-slate-500'); 
            targetBtn.classList.add('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-400'); 
        }
        
        const targetSub = document.getElementById(`sub-${catId}`);
        if (targetSub) {
            targetSub.classList.remove('hidden');
        }

        if (catId === 'ops') window.switchAdminTab('live');
        if (catId === 'players') window.switchAdminTab('players');
        if (catId === 'setup') window.switchAdminTab('schedules');
        if (catId === 'comms') window.switchAdminTab('notices');
        if (catId === 'system') window.switchAdminTab('audit');
    };

    window.switchAdminTab = function(tabId) {
        const allTabs = [
            'live', 'manual', 'history', 'date-errors', 'tournaments', 
            'players', 'diagnostics', 'schedules', 'team-editor', 'broadcast', 
            'sms-inbox', 'notices', 'community-mod', 'inbox-feedback', 'donations', 'audit', 'chat',
            'pending-accounts' // NEW TAB ADDED HERE
        ];

        allTabs.forEach(t => {
            const section = document.getElementById(`admin-${t}`);
            if (section) section.classList.add('hidden');
            
            const btn = document.getElementById(`tab-btn-${t}`);
            if (btn) btn.className = "px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-white cursor-pointer whitespace-nowrap transition-colors";
        });
        
        const targetSection = document.getElementById(`admin-${tabId}`);
        if (targetSection) targetSection.classList.remove('hidden');
        
        const targetBtn = document.getElementById(`tab-btn-${tabId}`);
        if (targetBtn) targetBtn.className = "px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold text-white bg-white/10 rounded-lg cursor-pointer whitespace-nowrap transition-colors";

        // Auto-Load Data for the selected tab
        if (tabId === 'inbox-feedback') window.loadPendingReports();
        if (tabId === 'date-errors') window.loadDateErrors();
        if (tabId === 'notices') window.loadAdminNotices();
        if (tabId === 'chat') window.loadAdminChat();
        if (tabId === 'donations') window.loadDonations();
        if (tabId === 'sms-inbox') window.loadSmsInbox();
        if (tabId === 'community-mod') window.loadCommunityMod();
        if (tabId === 'team-editor') window.loadTeams();
        if (tabId === 'pending-accounts') window.loadPendingAccounts();
        
        if (tabId === 'history') {
            const histDivFilter = document.getElementById('hist-div-filter');
            if (histDivFilter && histDivFilter.options.length <= 1) {
                fetch('/api/divisions')
                    .then(r => r.json())
                    .then(divs => { 
                        divs.forEach(d => { histDivFilter.innerHTML += `<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`; }); 
                    }).catch(e => console.error(e));
            }
        }
        
        if (['players', 'diagnostics', 'manual'].includes(tabId) && playerDirectoryData.length === 0) {
            window.loadPlayerDirectory();
        }
        
        if (tabId === 'players') window.loadChaosConfig();
        
        if (tabId === 'diagnostics') {
            fetch('/api/admin/get_rating_scales')
                .then(r => r.json())
                .then(d => {
                    document.getElementById('math-k-win').value = d.k_win; 
                    document.getElementById('math-k-loss').value = d.k_loss;
                }).catch(e => console.error(e));
        }
        
        if (tabId === 'audit') { 
            window.loadAuditLogs(); 
            window.loadAdminUsers(); 
            window.loadTrafficStats(); 
        }
    };

    window.forceRefresh = async function() {
        if (!confirm("Force the server to pull the latest data from the Master Google Sheet?")) return;
        const btn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="window.forceRefresh()"]');
        const originalHtml = btn ? btn.innerHTML : "FORCE REFRESH";
        
        if (btn) { 
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> SYNCING...'; 
            btn.disabled = true; 
        }
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/refresh', { method: 'POST' });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success || data.status === "Refreshed") {
                alert("✅ Sync triggered! Changes will appear momentarily."); 
            } else { 
                alert("❌ Sync failed."); 
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("❌ Network Error."); 
        } finally { 
            if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = originalHtml; btn.disabled = false; } 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // PLAYER SEARCH UTILITIES
    // ==========================================
    let playerDirectoryData = [];
    
    window.loadPlayerDirectory = async function() { 
        try { 
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/player_directory'); 
            playerDirectoryData = await res.json(); 
        } catch(e) {
            console.error("Failed to load player directory", e);
        } 
    };

    function attachPlayerSearch(inputId, suggId, hiddenId = null) {
        const input = document.getElementById(inputId); 
        const sugg = document.getElementById(suggId);
        
        if (!input || !sugg) return;
        
        input.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const q = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
            if (q.length < 1) { 
                sugg.classList.add('hidden'); 
                return; 
            }
            
            const matches = playerDirectoryData.filter(p => p.name.toLowerCase().includes(q));
            
            if (matches.length === 0) { 
                sugg.innerHTML = '<div class="px-3 py-2 text-slate-400 text-xs italic">No players found</div>'; 
                sugg.classList.remove('hidden'); 
                return; 
            }
            
            sugg.innerHTML = matches.slice(0, 8).map(p => `
                <div class="px-4 py-2 hover:bg-blue-600/30 cursor-pointer text-sm text-white font-bold border-b border-white/5" 
                     onclick="
                     document.getElementById('${inputId}').value = '${p.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}'; 
                     ${hiddenId ? `document.getElementById('${hiddenId}').value = '${p.id}';` : ''} 
                     document.getElementById('${suggId}').classList.add('hidden');
                     ${hiddenId === 'override-id' ? `window.fetchRatingContext('${p.id}');` : ''}
                     ">
                    ${p.name} <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono ml-2">${p.id}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            
            sugg.classList.remove('hidden');
        });
        
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => { 
            if (e.target !== input && e.target !== sugg) {
                sugg.classList.add('hidden'); 
            }
        });
    }

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        window.setAdminCategory('ops'); 
        attachPlayerSearch('override-search', 'override-suggestions', 'override-id');
        attachPlayerSearch('merge-bad-search', 'merge-bad-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('merge-good-search', 'merge-good-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('diag-p1-search', 'diag-p1-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('diag-p2-search', 'diag-p2-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('manual-p1', 'sugg-p1');
        attachPlayerSearch('manual-p2', 'sugg-p2');
    });

    // ==========================================
    // ACCOUNT LINKING APPROVALS
    // ==========================================
    window.loadPendingAccounts = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('pendingAccountsList');
        if (!list) return;
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl text-indigo-500"></i></div>';

        // Make sure we have the player directory loaded for the suggestion box
        if (playerDirectoryData.length === 0) await window.loadPlayerDirectory();

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/pending_accounts');
            const data = await res.json();

            if (data.length === 0) {
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-xl">Awesome! No pending accounts to approve.</div>';
                return;
            }

            let html = '';
            data.forEach(a => {
                html += `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 shadow-lg mb-3">
                    <div>
                        <div class="font-bold text-white text-lg">${a.name}</div>
                        <div class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono">${a.email} • DOB: ${a.dob}</div>
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono mt-1">UID: ${a.uid}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 bg-black/30 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 w-full md:w-auto">
                        <div class="relative w-full md:w-64">
                            <input type="text" id="link-search-${a.uid}" placeholder="Link to official player..." class="w-full bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-xs outline-none focus:border-indigo-500" autocomplete="off" value="${a.name}">
                            <div id="link-sugg-${a.uid}" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 top-full mt-1 bg-slate-700 rounded shadow-xl hidden border border-white/10 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar"></div>
                        </div>
                        <button onclick="window.linkAccount('${a.uid}')" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold py-2.5 px-4 rounded-lg text-xs transition shadow-lg whitespace-nowrap"><i class="fa-solid fa-link mr-1"></i> Approve</button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;

            data.forEach(a => { attachPlayerSearch(`link-search-${a.uid}`, `link-sugg-${a.uid}`); });
        } catch(e) {
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-400 text-center py-10">Error loading pending accounts.</div>';
        }
    };

    window.linkAccount = async function(uid) {
        const playerName = document.getElementById(`link-search-${uid}`).value;
        if (!playerName) return alert("Please select an official player name to link.");
        if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to officially link UID ${uid} to the Glicko profile for ${playerName}?`)) return;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/link_account', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ uid: uid, player_name: playerName })
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) {
                alert("✅ Account linked and approved! The player can now access their stats in the App.");
                window.loadPendingAccounts();
            } else {
                alert("❌ Failed to link account.");
            }
        } catch(e) {
            alert("Network Error");
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MANUAL MATCH & HISTORY
    // ==========================================
    window.submitManualMatch = async function() {
        const p1 = document.getElementById('manual-p1').value; 
        const p2 = document.getElementById('manual-p2').value;
        const date = document.getElementById('manual-date').value; 
        const scores = document.getElementById('manual-scores').value;
        
        if (!p1 || !p2 || !date) return alert("Player 1, Player 2, and Date are required.");
        if (!confirm(`Create official match record?\n\n${p1} vs ${p2}\nDate: ${date}\nScores: ${scores || 'None provided'}`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/manual_match', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, date: date, scores: scores }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert(`✅ Match injected successfully! The database is auto-syncing in the background.`); 
                document.getElementById('manual-p1').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('manual-p2').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('manual-scores').value = ''; 
            } else {
                alert("❌ Error injecting match.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network error."); 
        }
    };

    window.searchHistory = async function() {
        const q = document.getElementById('history-search').value.trim(); 
        const divFilterObj = document.getElementById('hist-div-filter');
        const sourceFilterObj = document.getElementById('hist-source-filter');
        
        const divFilter = divFilterObj ? divFilterObj.value : 'All'; 
        const sourceFilter = sourceFilterObj ? sourceFilterObj.value : 'All';
        
        const list = document.getElementById('historyList'); 
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-indigo-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/history?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}&source=${encodeURIComponent(sourceFilter)}`); 
            let matches = await res.json();
            
            if (divFilter !== 'All') {
                matches = matches.filter(m => m.division.toLowerCase() === divFilter.toLowerCase());
            }
            
            if (matches.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic">No matches found.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            let html = '';
            matches.forEach(m => {
                let gameHistoryHtml = '';
                if (m.game_history) {
                    gameHistoryHtml = `<div class="mt-3 bg-black/30 p-2 rounded border border-white/5 text-center text-xs font-mono text-slate-300">Set Scores: ${m.game_history}</div>`;
                } else if (m.rich_stats && m.rich_stats.total_duration) {
                    gameHistoryHtml = `<div class="mt-3 bg-blue-900/20 p-2 rounded border border-blue-500/20 text-center text-xs text-blue-300"><i class="fa-solid fa-tablet-screen-button"></i> iPad Match • Duration: ${m.rich_stats.total_duration}</div>`;
                }

                const sourceBadge = m.source === 'Spreadsheet' 
                    ? `<span class="bg-green-900/30 text-green-400 border border-green-500/20 text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-excel mr-1"></i>Sheet</span>` 
                    : `<span class="bg-blue-900/30 text-blue-400 border border-blue-500/20 text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner"><i class="fa-solid fa-tablet mr-1"></i>App</span>`;

                html += `
                <div class="bg-black/30 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 mb-3 flex flex-col hover:bg-slate-800 transition-colors">
                    <div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 w-full">
                        <div class="flex-1 w-full">
                            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                                <span class="bg-slate-800 text-slate-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-mono border border-white/10">ID: ${m.match_id || 'N/A'}</span>
                                <span class="bg-indigo-900/30 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">${m.division}</span>
                                ${sourceBadge}
                            </div>
                            <div class="text-lg font-black text-white">${m.p1} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-sm">vs</span> ${m.p2}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-slate-900/80 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/10 w-full md:w-auto shrink-0">
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-14">
                                <span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Score 1</span>
                                <input type="number" id="s1-${m.id}" value="${m.s1}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm">
                            </div>
                            <span class="text-slate-600 font-black mt-3">-</span>
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-14">
                                <span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Score 2</span>
                                <input type="number" id="s2-${m.id}" value="${m.s2}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm">
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-28 ml-2">
                                <span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Date</span>
                                <input type="text" id="date-${m.id}" value="${m.date}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm">
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex flex-col gap-1 ml-2 mt-4">
                                <button onclick="window.adminSaveHistoryEdit('${m.p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.date}', '${m.id}')" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition shadow-lg flex items-center justify-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-floppy-disk"></i></button>
                                <button onclick="document.getElementById('data-${m.match_id}').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="bg-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-600 text-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition shadow-lg flex items-center justify-center" title="View Match Data"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-simple"></i></button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div id="data-${m.match_id}" class="hidden w-full mt-4 bg-black/40 border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-4 flex-col gap-3">
                        <div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <div class="bg-slate-800 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5 relative overflow-hidden">
                                <div class="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 ${m.p1_delta > 0 ? 'bg-green-500' : 'bg-red-500'}"></div>
                                <div class="text-sky-400 font-bold mb-1 border-b border-white/10 pb-1 pl-3">${m.p1}</div>
                                <div class="text-sm text-slate-300 font-mono mt-2 pl-3">Rating: ${Math.round(m.p1_before)} <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right text-slate-600 mx-1 text-[10px]"></i> ${Math.round(m.p1_after)} <span class="${m.p1_delta > 0 ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'} ml-1 text-xs">(${m.p1_delta > 0 ? '+' : ''}${Math.round(m.p1_delta)})</span></div>
                                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 font-mono mt-1 pl-3">RD: ±${Math.round(m.p1_rd_before)} <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right mx-1 text-[10px]"></i> ±${Math.round(m.p1_rd_after)}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="bg-slate-800 p-3 rounded-lg border border-white/5 relative overflow-hidden">
                                <div class="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 ${m.p2_delta > 0 ? 'bg-green-500' : 'bg-red-500'}"></div>
                                <div class="text-red-400 font-bold mb-1 border-b border-white/10 pb-1 pl-3">${m.p2}</div>
                                <div class="text-sm text-slate-300 font-mono mt-2 pl-3">Rating: ${Math.round(m.p2_before)} <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right text-slate-600 mx-1 text-[10px]"></i> ${Math.round(m.p2_after)} <span class="${m.p2_delta > 0 ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'} ml-1 text-xs">(${m.p2_delta > 0 ? '+' : ''}${Math.round(m.p2_delta)})</span></div>
                                <div class="text-xs text-slate-500 font-mono mt-1 pl-3">RD: ±${Math.round(m.p2_rd_before)} <i class="fa-solid fa-arrow-right mx-1 text-[10px]"></i> ±${Math.round(m.p2_rd_after)}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        ${gameHistoryHtml}
                        
                        <div class="mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-white/10 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center justify-between gap-3">
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-yellow-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest"><i class="fa-solid fa-wrench mr-1"></i> Override Point Changes</div>
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                <input type="number" step="0.1" id="override-p1-${m.match_id}" placeholder="${m.p1} pts" class="w-24 bg-black/40 border border-white/10 text-white text-center rounded py-1.5 text-xs focus:ring-1 focus:ring-yellow-500 outline-none" value="${m.p1_delta ? Math.round(m.p1_delta) : ''}">
                                <input type="number" step="0.1" id="override-p2-${m.match_id}" placeholder="${m.p2} pts" class="w-24 bg-black/40 border border-white/10 text-white text-center rounded py-1.5 text-xs focus:ring-1 focus:ring-yellow-500 outline-none" value="${m.p2_delta ? Math.round(m.p2_delta) : ''}">
                                <button onclick="window.saveDeltaOverride('${m.match_id}', '${m.p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="bg-yellow-600 hover:bg-yellow-500 text-black font-black px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs transition shadow-lg">SAVE</button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) { 
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-400 text-center py-10">Error loading history.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.saveDeltaOverride = async function(matchId, p1, p2) {
        const p1Delta = document.getElementById(`override-p1-${matchId}`).value; 
        const p2Delta = document.getElementById(`override-p2-${matchId}`).value;
        
        if (!p1Delta || !p2Delta) return alert("Please enter point changes for both players.");
        if (!confirm(`OVERRIDE MATH:\n\nForce ${p1} to get ${p1Delta} pts\nForce ${p2} to get ${p2Delta} pts\n\nProceed?`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/override_deltas', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ match_id: matchId, p1_delta: p1Delta, p2_delta: p2Delta }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert("✅ Point overrides saved!"); 
                window.searchHistory(); 
            } else { 
                alert("❌ Failed to save."); 
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    window.adminSaveHistoryEdit = async function(p1, p2, oldDate, id) {
        const s1 = document.getElementById(`s1-${id}`).value; 
        const s2 = document.getElementById(`s2-${id}`).value; 
        const newDate = document.getElementById(`date-${id}`).value;
        
        if (!confirm(`OVERRIDE MATCH:\n\nPlayers: ${p1} vs ${p2}\nNew Score: ${s1}-${s2}\nNew Date: ${newDate}\n\nProceed?`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/update_match', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, date: oldDate, s1: s1, s2: s2, new_date: newDate }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) {
                alert("✅ Update locked in!"); 
            } else {
                alert("❌ Failed to update match.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MISSING DATE FIXER
    // ==========================================
    window.loadDateErrors = async function() {
        const dList = document.getElementById('dateErrorsList'); 
        const dBadge = document.getElementById('date-badge');
        if (!dList) return; 
        
        dList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-orange-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/date_errors'); 
            const errors = await res.json();
            
            if (dBadge) { 
                dBadge.innerText = errors.length; 
                errors.length > 0 ? dBadge.classList.remove('hidden') : dBadge.classList.add('hidden'); 
            }
            
            if (errors.length === 0) { 
                dList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-600 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-xl">Awesome! No missing dates found.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            let html = "";
            errors.forEach(m => {
                html += `
                <div id="date-card-${m.id}" class="date-card bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 shadow-lg mb-3" data-season="${m.season}" data-div="${m.division}" data-week="${m.week}">
                    <div class="flex-1 w-full">
                        <div class="flex flex-wrap gap-2 items-center mb-2">
                            <span class="bg-red-900/30 text-red-400 border border-red-500/20 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest px-2 py-0.5 rounded">NO DATE</span>
                            <span class="bg-indigo-900/30 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest px-2 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-excel mr-1"></i>${m.sheet_name} • ROW ${m.row_index}</span>
                            <span class="bg-yellow-900/30 text-yellow-400 border border-yellow-500/20 text-[10px] font-bold tracking-widest px-2 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner uppercase">${m.division} • WK ${m.week}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="font-black text-white text-lg">${m.home_players[0]} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-sm">vs</span> ${m.away_players[0]}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-black/30 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shrink-0">
                        <div class="flex flex-col">
                            <span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1">Fix Date (DD/MM/YYYY)</span>
                            <input type="text" id="fix-date-${m.id}" placeholder="e.g. 14/02/2026" class="w-28 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1 focus:border-orange-500 focus:outline-none text-xs">
                        </div>
                        <button onclick="window.adminBulkDateFix('${m.season}', '${m.division}', '${m.week}', '${m.id}', this)" class="bg-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold py-2 px-4 rounded text-xs transition-transform hover:scale-105 shadow-[0_0_10px_rgba(249,115,22,0.4)] mt-3">FIX</button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            dList.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) { 
            dList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-400 text-center py-10">Error loading date errors.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.adminBulkDateFix = async function(season, division, week, id, btnElement) {
        const newDate = document.getElementById(`fix-date-${id}`).value;
        if (!newDate) return alert("Please enter a valid date.");
        
        btnElement.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i>'; 
        btnElement.disabled = true;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/bulk_fix_date', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ season: season, division: division, week: week, date: newDate }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                const allCards = document.querySelectorAll('.date-card'); 
                let removedCount = 0;
                allCards.forEach(card => {
                    if (card.dataset.season === season && card.dataset.div === division && card.dataset.week === week) {
                        card.style.transition = "all 0.3s ease"; 
                        card.style.opacity = "0"; 
                        card.style.transform = "translateX(20px)"; 
                        setTimeout(() => card.remove(), 300); 
                        removedCount++;
                    }
                });
                
                const dBadge = document.getElementById('date-badge');
                if (dBadge) { 
                    let count = parseInt(dBadge.innerText) || 0; 
                    count = Math.max(0, count - removedCount); 
                    dBadge.innerText = count; 
                    if (count === 0) { 
                        dBadge.classList.add('hidden'); 
                        document.getElementById('dateErrorsList').innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-600 text-center py-10 italic">Awesome! No missing dates found.</div>'; 
                    } 
                }
            } else { 
                alert("❌ Failed to set bulk date fix."); 
                btnElement.innerHTML = 'FIX'; 
                btnElement.disabled = false; 
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
            btnElement.innerHTML = 'FIX'; 
            btnElement.disabled = false; 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // PDF PARSER & TEAM ROSTER EDITOR
    // ==========================================
    window.uploadPdfSchedule = async function() {
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('pdf-file-upload'); 
        const seasonInput = document.getElementById('pdf-season'); 
        const divInput = document.getElementById('pdf-division'); 
        const btn = document.getElementById('pdf-upload-btn');
        
        if (!fileInput.files.length) return alert("Please select a PDF file first.");
        if (!seasonInput.value) return alert("Please specify the Season (e.g., Summer 2026).");
        if (!divInput.value) return alert("Please specify the Division.");
        
        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('pdf', fileInput.files[0]); 
        formData.append('season', seasonInput.value);
        formData.append('division', divInput.value);
        
        const originalText = btn.innerHTML; 
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> PARSING PDF & EXTRACTING TEAMS...'; 
        btn.disabled = true;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/upload_schedule', { method: 'POST', body: formData });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert(`✅ Success! AI extracted ${data.teams_found} teams and ${data.matches_found} matchups from the PDF.`); 
                fileInput.value = ''; 
                divInput.value = ''; 
                seasonInput.value = '';
                
                if (document.getElementById('admin-team-editor') && !document.getElementById('admin-team-editor').classList.contains('hidden')) {
                    window.loadTeams();
                }
            } else {
                alert(`❌ Parsing Error: ${data.error}`);
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        } finally { 
            btn.innerHTML = originalText; 
            btn.disabled = false; 
        }
    };

    window.loadTeams = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('teamsList');
        if (!list) return;
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full text-center py-10"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl text-emerald-500"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/teams'); 
            const teams = await res.json();
            
            if (teams.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full text-center text-slate-500 py-10 italic">No teams found. Upload a schedule PDF first to auto-extract teams!</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            let html = '';
            teams.forEach(t => {
                const pInputs = [0, 1, 2].map(i => {
                    const pName = t.players && t.players[i] ? t.players[i] : '';
                    return `<input type="text" id="team-${t.id}-p${i}" value="${pName.replace(/"/g, '&quot;')}" placeholder="Player ${i+1}" class="w-full bg-black/40 border border-white/10 rounded px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white mb-2 focus:border-emerald-500 outline-none">`;
                }).join('');
                
                html += `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shadow-lg relative overflow-hidden">
                    <div class="absolute left-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-1 bg-emerald-500"></div>
                    <div class="pl-3">
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-emerald-400 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest mb-1">${t.season || 'Unknown Season'} • ${t.division || 'Unknown Division'}</div>
                        <h3 class="text-white font-black text-lg mb-4 pb-2 border-b border-white/10">${t.team_name || t.id}</h3>
                        <div class="space-y-1 mb-4">${pInputs}</div>
                        <button onclick="window.saveTeam('${t.id}')" class="w-full bg-emerald-600 hover:bg-emerald-500 text-white font-bold py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm transition shadow-[0_0_10px_rgba(16,185,129,0.3)]">Save Roster</button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) { 
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="col-span-full text-red-500 text-center py-10">Error loading teams.</div>'; 
        }
    };
    
    window.saveTeam = async function(teamId) {
        const players = [];
        for(let i=0; i<3; i++) { 
            const val = document.getElementById(`team-${teamId}-p${i}`).value.trim(); 
            if (val) players.push(val); 
        }
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/update_team', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ team_id: teamId, players: players }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert("✅ Team saved successfully!"); 
            } else { 
                alert("❌ Error saving team."); 
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // PLAYER EDITOR & RATING OVERRIDES
    // ==========================================
    window.fetchRatingContext = async function(playerId) {
        const contextDiv = document.getElementById('override-context');
        if (!contextDiv) return;
        
        contextDiv.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Loading recent rating context...';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/rating_context/${playerId}`);
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if (data.length === 0) {
                contextDiv.innerHTML = '<div class="italic">No recent match history found for this player.</div>';
                return;
            }
            
            let html = '<div class="font-bold text-white mb-2 pb-1 border-b border-white/10"><i class="fa-solid fa-clock-rotate-left mr-2"></i>Last 6 Match Ratings:</div>';
            data.forEach(m => {
                html += `<div class="flex justify-between items-center py-1 border-b border-white/5 last:border-0"><span class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">${m.date} vs ${m.opponent}</span> <span class="text-emerald-400 font-mono font-bold">${m.rating}</span></div>`;
            });
            
            contextDiv.innerHTML = `<div class="bg-black/30 p-3 rounded border border-white/5 shadow-inner">${html}</div>`;
        } catch(e) {
            contextDiv.innerHTML = '';
        }
    };

    window.submitRatingOverride = async function() {
        const id = document.getElementById('override-id').value; 
        const rating = document.getElementById('override-score').value; 
        const isRetro = document.getElementById('override-retro').checked;
        
        if (!id || !rating) return alert("Please select a player and provide a rating.");
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/override_rating', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ player_id: id, rating: rating, retroactive: isRetro }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if (data.success) { 
                alert(`✅ Successfully applied rating override.`); 
                document.getElementById('override-id').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('override-search').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('override-score').value = ''; 
                if (document.getElementById('override-context')) document.getElementById('override-context').innerHTML = '';
            } else {
                alert("❌ Error applying rating override.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network error."); 
        }
    };
    
    window.bulkSetRatings = async function() {
        if (!confirm("⚠️ Are you sure you want to pull ALL ratings from the 'Ratings crap' sheet and apply them as of today?")) return;
        const btn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="window.bulkSetRatings()"]'); 
        const originalHtml = btn ? btn.innerHTML : "SET RATINGS";
        
        if (btn) { 
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> PULLING RATINGS...'; 
            btn.disabled = true; 
        }
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/bulk_pull_ratings', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({}) 
            });
            const text = await res.text(); 
            let data;
            try { 
                data = JSON.parse(text); 
            } catch(err) { 
                alert("Server Crash!"); 
                return; 
            }
            if (data.success) { 
                alert(`✅ Successfully imported ${data.count} ratings!`); 
                window.loadPlayerDirectory(); 
            } else {
                alert(`❌ Failed: ${data.error}`);
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network error: " + e.message); 
        } finally { 
            if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = originalHtml; btn.disabled = false; } 
        }
    };

    window.submitPlayerMerge = async function() {
        const bad = document.getElementById('merge-bad-search').value; 
        const good = document.getElementById('merge-good-search').value;
        
        if (!bad || !good) return alert("Please select both names.");
        if (bad.toLowerCase() === good.toLowerCase()) return alert("Names must be different.");
        if (!confirm(`⚠️ DANGER: You are about to PERMANENTLY merge "${bad}" into "${good}". Proceed?`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/merge', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ bad_name: bad, good_name: good }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert(`✅ Successfully merged profiles!`); 
                document.getElementById('merge-bad-search').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('merge-good-search').value = ''; 
            } else {
                alert("❌ Error merging players.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network error."); 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // SYSTEM MATH & DIAGNOSTICS
    // ==========================================
    window.saveMathMultipliers = async function() {
        const kWin = document.getElementById('math-k-win').value;
        const kLoss = document.getElementById('math-k-loss').value;
        if (!confirm(`WARNING: Changing these scales triggers a recalculation of the entire database.\n\nNew Win Scale: ${kWin}x\nNew Loss Scale: ${kLoss}x\n\nProceed?`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/set_rating_scales', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ k_win: kWin, k_loss: kLoss }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert("✅ Math parameters updated! The server is recalculating history."); 
                window.location.reload(); 
            } else {
                alert("❌ Error saving parameters.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    window.runDiagnostics = async function() {
        const p1 = document.getElementById('diag-p1-search').value; 
        const p2 = document.getElementById('diag-p2-search').value; 
        const s1 = document.getElementById('diag-s1').value; 
        const s2 = document.getElementById('diag-s2').value;
        const resultsBox = document.getElementById('diag-results'); 
        const btn = document.getElementById('diag-btn');
        
        if (!p1 || !p2) return alert("Please select both players.");
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Calculating...';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/glicko_calc', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, s1: s1, s2: s2 }) 
            });
            const d = await res.json();
            if (d.success) {
                const math = d.data;
                const renderPlayerMath = (pData) => {
                    const deltaColor = pData.delta > 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400";
                    const deltaSign = pData.delta > 0 ? "+" : "";
                    return `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-white/5 relative">
                        <div class="font-black text-white text-lg mb-4 border-b border-white/10 pb-2">${pData.name}</div>
                        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <div>
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1">Current Rating</div>
                                <div class="text-xl font-mono text-white">${pData.old_rating} <span class="text-xs text-slate-500">(±${pData.old_rd})</span></div>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1">Expected Win %</div>
                                <div class="text-xl font-mono text-sky-400">${pData.expected_win_pct}%</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/10 flex justify-between items-center bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg">
                            <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500">Calculated Shift</div>
                            <div class="text-2xl font-black font-mono ${deltaColor}">${deltaSign}${pData.delta} pts</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-center mt-3">
                            <span class="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-500 font-bold">Resulting Rating: </span>
                            <span class="text-white font-mono font-bold">${pData.new_rating}</span>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                };
                resultsBox.innerHTML = `<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">${renderPlayerMath(math.p1)}${renderPlayerMath(math.p2)}</div>`;
                resultsBox.classList.remove('hidden');
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        } finally { 
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-microchip"></i> Run Simulation'; 
        }
    };

    window.loadChaosConfig = async function() {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/chaos_config'); 
            const data = await res.json();
            
            const req = data.req || 3; 
            const current = data.approvals ? data.approvals.length : 0; 
            const pct = Math.min(100, (current / req) * 100);
            
            const countEl = document.getElementById('chaos-vote-count'); 
            if (countEl) countEl.innerText = `${current}/${req}`;
            
            const prog = document.getElementById('chaos-progress-bar'); 
            if (prog) prog.style.width = `${pct}%`;
            
            const votersList = document.getElementById('chaos-voters-list'); 
            if (votersList) { 
                if (data.approvals && data.approvals.length > 0) votersList.innerText = `Voters: ${data.approvals.join(', ')}`; 
                else votersList.innerText = "Waiting for signatures..."; 
            }
            
            const weeksInput = document.getElementById('chaos-weeks'); 
            if (weeksInput && data.weeks && data.weeks.length > 0) weeksInput.value = data.weeks.join(', ');
            
            const banner = document.getElementById('chaos-status-banner');
            if (banner) {
                if (data.active) {
                    banner.className = "bg-red-900/30 border border-red-500/30 text-red-400 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold flex items-center gap-2 mb-4 animate-pulse";
                    banner.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-fire"></i> CHAOS MODE ARMED & ACTIVE';
                    document.getElementById('chaos-progress-bar').classList.remove('bg-red-500'); 
                    document.getElementById('chaos-progress-bar').classList.add('bg-red-500', 'shadow-[0_0_10px_rgba(239,68,68,0.8)]');
                } else {
                    banner.className = "bg-green-900/30 border border-green-500/30 text-green-400 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold flex items-center gap-2 mb-4";
                    banner.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-lock"></i> Anti-Riot is ON (Default Safe Mode)';
                }
            }
        } catch(e) { }
    };
    
    window.castChaosVote = async function() {
        const weeksRaw = document.getElementById('chaos-weeks').value;
        if (!weeksRaw) return alert("You must specify which weeks to apply Chaos Mode to.");
        const weeks = weeksRaw.split(',').map(w => w.trim()).filter(w => w.length > 0);
        if (!confirm(`Authorize Chaos Mode for: ${weeks.join(', ')}?`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/chaos_vote', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ weeks: weeks }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) window.loadChaosConfig(); 
            else alert("Failed to record signature.");
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };
    
    window.clearChaosVotes = async function() {
        if (!confirm("Revoke all approvals and restore Anti-Riot lock?")) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/chaos_clear', { method: 'POST' });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                document.getElementById('chaos-weeks').value = ''; 
                window.loadChaosConfig(); 
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // COMMUNITY FORUM MODERATION
    // ==========================================
    window.loadCommunityMod = async function() {
        const feed = document.getElementById('mod-forum-feed');
        if (!feed) return;
        feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-red-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/hub/forum');
            const posts = await res.json();
            
            if (posts.length === 0) { 
                feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center text-slate-500 py-10 italic">No posts in the community yet.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            feed.innerHTML = posts.map(p => `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex justify-between items-start gap-4">
                    <div class="flex-1">
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 mb-1 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest"><span class="text-white">${p.author_name}</span> • ${p.time_str}</div>
                        <div class="text-sm text-slate-300 whitespace-pre-wrap">${p.content}</div>
                        ${p.image_url ? `<img src="${p.image_url}" class="mt-3 h-24 rounded object-cover shadow-lg border border-white/10">` : ''}
                    </div>
                    <button onclick="window.deleteCommunityPost('${p.id}')" class="bg-red-900/40 hover:bg-red-600 text-red-500 hover:text-white px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition shrink-0 border border-red-500/20"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch(e) { 
            feed.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-500 py-10 text-center">Error loading feed.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.deleteCommunityPost = async function(id) {
        if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to permanently delete this post?")) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/delete_post', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: {'Content-Type':'application/json'}, 
                body: JSON.stringify({post_id: id}) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert("Post deleted."); 
                window.loadCommunityMod(); 
            } else { 
                alert("Failed to delete post."); 
            }
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    // ==========================================
    // NOTICES, SMS INBOX, AND FEEDBACK
    // ==========================================
    window.loadPendingReports = async function() {
        const fList = document.getElementById('feedbackList'); 
        if (!fList) return; 
        fList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-slate-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/reports'); 
            const reports = await res.json(); 
            let fHtml = ""; 
            
            reports.forEach(r => {
                if (r.type === 'FEEDBACK') {
                    fHtml += `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-lg border border-blue-500/20 shadow-lg mb-3">
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-start mb-2">
                            <div>
                                <span class="text-xs font-bold text-blue-400 bg-blue-900/30 px-2 py-1 rounded border border-blue-500/20 mr-2">${r.title}</span>
