                                <span class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono">${r.date}</span>
                            </div>
                            <div class="text-xs text-slate-500">From: <span class="text-slate-300 font-bold">${r.reporter}</span></div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 rounded p-3 mb-3 whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-slate-300">${r.problem}</div>
                        <div class="flex gap-2 border-t border-white/5 pt-3">
                            <button onclick="window.resolveReport('${r.id}', 'approve')" class="flex-1 bg-green-600 hover:bg-green-500 text-white font-bold py-2 px-4 rounded text-sm transition-colors shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-check mr-1"></i> Mark Resolved</button>
                            <button onclick="window.resolveReport('${r.id}', 'reject')" class="flex-1 bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-500 text-white font-bold py-2 px-4 rounded text-sm transition-colors shadow-lg"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash mr-1"></i> Dismiss</button>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }
            });
            fList.innerHTML = fHtml || '<div class="text-slate-600 text-center py-10 italic">No new feedback.</div>';
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.resolveReport = async function(id, action) {
        if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to ${action} this?`)) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/resolve', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ report_id: id, action: action }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { window.loadPendingReports(); } 
            else alert("Error resolving item.");
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network error."); 
        }
    };

    window.loadAdminNotices = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('adminNoticesList'); 
        if (!list) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/notices'); 
            const notices = await res.json();
            if (notices.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-600 text-center py-10 italic">No active notices.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            list.innerHTML = notices.map(n => {
                let badgeColor = 'bg-slate-700 text-slate-300';
                if (n.type === 'Update') badgeColor = 'bg-sky-500/20 text-sky-400 border border-sky-500/30';
                if (n.type === 'Event') badgeColor = 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-400 border border-yellow-500/30';
                if (n.type === 'Alert') badgeColor = 'bg-red-500/20 text-red-400 border border-red-500/30';
                return `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex justify-between items-start gap-4">
                    <div>
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                            <span class="text-[10px] font-bold px-2 py-0.5 rounded uppercase tracking-widest ${badgeColor}">${n.type}</span>
                            <span class="text-xs text-emerald-400 font-mono">${n.date_str}</span>
                        </div>
                        <h4 class="text-white font-bold text-lg leading-tight mb-2">${n.title}</h4>
                        <p class="text-sm text-slate-400 line-clamp-2">${n.message}</p>
                    </div>
                    <button onclick="window.deleteNotice('${n.id}')" class="bg-red-900/30 hover:bg-red-600 text-red-500 hover:text-white border border-red-500/20 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg transition-colors shrink-0"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
                </div>`;
            }).join('');
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.submitNotice = async function() {
        const title = document.getElementById('notice-title').value; 
        const type = document.getElementById('notice-type').value; 
        const msg = document.getElementById('notice-message').value;
        if (!title || !msg) return alert("Title and Message are required.");
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/add_notice', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ title: title, type: type, message: msg }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                document.getElementById('notice-title').value = ''; 
                document.getElementById('notice-message').value = ''; 
                window.loadAdminNotices(); 
                alert("✅ Notice posted to public site!"); 
            } else {
                alert("❌ Failed to post notice.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    window.deleteNotice = async function(id) {
        if (!confirm("Remove this notice from the public site?")) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/delete_notice', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ notice_id: id }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) window.loadAdminNotices(); 
            else alert("Failed to delete notice.");
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.loadSmsInbox = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('smsInboxList'); 
        if (!list) return;
        
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-pink-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/sms_inbox'); 
            const messages = await res.json();
            
            if (messages.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-8 italic border border-white/5 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-xl">No replies received yet.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            list.innerHTML = messages.map(m => `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-lg border border-pink-500/20 shadow">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2 border-b border-white/5 pb-2">
                        <span class="text-xs font-mono font-bold text-pink-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-mobile-screen-button mr-2"></i>${m.from}</span>
                        <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono">${m.time_str}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-sm text-slate-200 font-bold">${m.body}</div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch(e) { 
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-500 text-center py-8 italic">Failed to load SMS inbox.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.loadAdminChat = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('adminChatList'); 
        if (!list) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/messages'); 
            const messages = await res.json();
            if (messages.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-8 italic">No notes yet.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            list.innerHTML = messages.map(m => `
                <div class="bg-slate-900/50 p-4 rounded-lg border border-white/5 relative">
                    <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-2 border-b border-white/5 pb-2">
                        <span class="text-xs font-bold text-indigo-400"><i class="fa-solid fa-user-shield mr-1"></i>${m.author}</span>
                        <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono">${m.time_str}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-sm text-slate-300 whitespace-pre-wrap">${m.message}</div>
                </div>
            `).join('');
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.postAdminMessage = async function() {
        const input = document.getElementById('admin-chat-input'); 
        const msg = input.value.trim(); 
        if (!msg) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/add_message', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ message: msg }) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                input.value = ''; 
                window.loadAdminChat(); 
            } else {
                alert("Failed to post message.");
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // SYSTEM AUDIT & DONATIONS
    // ==========================================
    window.loadDonations = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('donationsList'); 
        const totalEl = document.getElementById('donations-total'); 
        const countEl = document.getElementById('donations-count');
        if (!list) return;
        
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-emerald-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/donations'); 
            const data = await res.json();
            let total = 0; 
            let html = '';
            
            if (data.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic">No donations recorded yet.</div>'; 
                if (totalEl) totalEl.innerText = '$0.00'; 
                if (countEl) countEl.innerText = '0'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            data.forEach(d => {
                total += d.amount;
                html += `
                <div class="bg-black/30 p-4 rounded-xl border border-emerald-500/20 flex justify-between items-center transition-colors hover:bg-slate-800">
                    <div>
                        <div class="font-bold text-white text-lg">${d.name}</div>
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono tracking-widest mt-1">${d.time_str}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-2xl font-black text-emerald-400 font-mono bg-emerald-900/20 px-3 py-1 rounded-lg border border-emerald-500/30">$${d.amount.toFixed(2)}</div>
                </div>`;
            });
            
            list.innerHTML = html;
            if (totalEl) totalEl.innerText = '$' + total.toFixed(2); 
            if (countEl) countEl.innerText = data.length;
        } catch (e) { 
            list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-400 text-center py-10">Error loading donations.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.loadTrafficStats = async function() {
        const viewsEl = document.getElementById('dash-traffic-views'); 
        const uniquesEl = document.getElementById('dash-traffic-uniques');
        if (!viewsEl || !uniquesEl) return;
        try { 
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/traffic'); 
            const data = await res.json(); 
            viewsEl.innerText = data.views; 
            uniquesEl.innerText = data.uniques; 
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.loadAuditLogs = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('auditLogList'); 
        if (!list) return;
        const filterObj = document.getElementById('audit-filter');
        const filter = filterObj ? filterObj.value : 'ALL';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/audit_logs'); 
            const logs = await res.json();
            
            if (logs.length === 0) { 
                list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 py-10 text-center italic">No actions recorded yet.</div>'; 
                return; 
            }
            
            let html = '';
            logs.forEach(l => {
                if (filter === 'MATCH' && !['UPDATE_MATCH', 'ADD_MATCH', 'FORCE_FINISH_LIVE', 'OVERRIDE_DELTAS'].includes(l.action)) return;
                if (filter === 'RATING' && !['OVERRIDE_RATING', 'UPDATE_MATH', 'BULK_IMPORT_RATINGS'].includes(l.action)) return;
                if (filter === 'SYSTEM' && !['SESSION_START', 'SESSION_END', 'FORCE_REFRESH'].includes(l.action)) return;

                const isUndone = l.status === 'undone'; 
                const bgClass = isUndone ? 'bg-slate-800/30 border-dashed opacity-50' : 'bg-slate-800';
                const noUndoActions = ['MERGE_PLAYER', 'ADD_NOTICE', 'DELETE_NOTICE', 'SET_FORMAT', 'FORCE_REFRESH', 'RESOLVE_INBOX', 'SMS_BROADCAST', 'SESSION_START', 'SESSION_END', 'APPROVE_ACCOUNT'];
                const undoBtn = (!isUndone && !noUndoActions.includes(l.action)) 
                    ? `<button onclick="window.undoAction('${l.id}')" class="text-[10px] bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-500 text-white font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded transition ml-auto shadow">UNDO</button>` 
                    : '';
                
                html += `
                <div class="${bgClass} border border-white/5 p-3 rounded-lg flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center gap-3">
                    <div class="flex flex-col gap-1">
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                            <span class="text-[9px] bg-slate-700 text-white px-2 py-0.5 rounded uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">${l.action}</span>
                            <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-mono">${l.time_str}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-sm font-bold text-white">${l.description}</div>
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500">Authorized by: <span class="text-slate-300">${l.admin}</span></div>
                    </div>
                    ${undoBtn}
                    ${isUndone ? `<div class="ml-auto text-[10px] text-red-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest border border-red-500/30 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-red-900/20">REVERSED BY ${l.undone_by}</div>` : ''}
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html || '<div class="text-slate-500 py-10 text-center italic">No logs match this filter.</div>';
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.undoAction = async function(logId) {
        if (!confirm("Are you sure you want to completely reverse this action?")) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/undo_action', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, 
                body: JSON.stringify({log_id: logId}) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { 
                alert("✅ Action successfully undone!"); 
                window.loadAuditLogs(); 
            } else { 
                alert("❌ Failed to undo action."); 
            }
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.loadAdminUsers = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('adminUsersList'); 
        if (!list) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/users'); 
            const users = await res.json(); 
            let html = '';
            
            users.forEach(u => {
                const isPending = u.role === 'pending'; 
                const isTemp = u.role === 'temp_super_admin';
                let roleBadge = '';
                
                if (isPending) {
                    roleBadge = '<span class="text-yellow-500 bg-yellow-900/30 border border-yellow-500/30 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] uppercase font-bold">Pending</span>';
                } else if (isTemp) {
                    roleBadge = `<span class="text-pink-400 bg-pink-900/30 border border-pink-500/30 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] uppercase font-bold">Temp Super Admin <i class="fa-solid fa-clock text-[8px] ml-1"></i> ${u.expires_at_str}</span>`;
                } else {
                    roleBadge = `<span class="text-blue-400 bg-blue-900/30 border border-blue-500/30 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[9px] uppercase font-bold">${u.role}</span>`;
                }
                
                let actions = '';
                if (u.role !== 'super_admin') {
                    if (isPending) { 
                        actions = `
                        <button onclick="window.manageUser('${u.email}', 'approve')" class="text-green-500 hover:text-green-400 text-sm mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-check"></i></button>
                        <button onclick="window.manageUser('${u.email}', 'delete')" class="text-red-500 hover:text-red-400 text-sm mx-1"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>`; 
                    } else { 
                        actions = `<button onclick="window.manageUser('${u.email}', 'revoke')" class="text-red-400 hover:text-red-300 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase border border-red-500/30 px-2 py-1 rounded">Revoke Access</button>`; 
                        if (u.role === 'admin') {
                            actions += `<button onclick="window.manageUser('${u.email}', 'temp_super')" class="ml-2 text-pink-400 hover:text-pink-300 text-[10px] font-bold uppercase border border-pink-500/30 px-2 py-1 rounded">+ 7 Day Super Admin</button>`;
                        }
                    }
                }
                
                html += `
                <div class="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 p-3 rounded-lg flex flex-col md:flex-row md:items-center justify-between gap-3">
                    <div>
                        <div class="text-sm font-bold text-white mb-1 truncate" title="${u.email}">${u.email}</div>
                        ${roleBadge}
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3">${actions}</div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) {}
    }

    window.manageUser = async function(email, action) {
        if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to apply this access rule for ${email}?`)) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/approve_user', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'}, 
                body: JSON.stringify({email: email, action: action}) 
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) window.loadAdminUsers();
        } catch(e) {}
    }
</script>

<script type="module">
    import { initializeApp } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-app.js";
    import { getFirestore, collection, query, onSnapshot } from "https://www.gstatic.com/firebasejs/10.7.1/firebase-firestore.js";

    const firebaseConfig = { 
        apiKey: "AIzaSyDq05wFsKLHtt8G0Z5yLOG9pIk9UX24S4o", 
        authDomain: "gctta-stats-live.firebaseapp.com", 
        projectId: "gctta-stats-live", 
        storageBucket: "gctta-stats-live.firebasestorage.app", 
        messagingSenderId: "1070856258556", 
        appId: "1:1070856258556:web:be438e04c1941abc3c6879" 
    };
    
    try {
        const app = initializeApp(firebaseConfig);
        const db = getFirestore(app);

        window.setFormatOverride = async function(fixtureId, formatType) {
            try { 
                await fetch('/api/admin/set_fixture_format', { 
                    method: 'POST', 
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ fixture_id: fixtureId, format_type: formatType }) 
                }); 
            } catch(e) {}
        };

        onSnapshot(query(collection(db, "fixture_schedule")), (snapshot) => {
            const liveList = document.getElementById("live-list"); 
            const scheduledList = document.getElementById("scheduled-list");
            let liveCount = 0; 
            let liveHtml = ""; 
            let schedHtml = "";
            
            snapshot.forEach((doc) => {
                const m = doc.data(); 
                const id = doc.id;
                const p1 = (m.home_players && m.home_players.length > 0) ? m.home_players[0] : m.home_team;
                const p2 = (m.away_players && m.away_players.length > 0) ? m.away_players[0] : m.away_team;
                
                if (m.match_status === "Live" || m.match_status === "Paused" || m.live_home_score > 0 || m.live_away_score > 0) {
                    liveCount++; 
                    const s1 = m.live_home_sets || 0; 
                    const s2 = m.live_away_sets || 0;
                    
                    liveHtml += `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-blue-500/30 shadow-lg relative overflow-hidden mb-4">
                        <div class="absolute top-0 right-0 bg-blue-500 text-white text-[9px] font-black uppercase tracking-widest px-3 py-1 rounded-bl-lg animate-pulse">ACTIVE NOW</div>
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-center mb-3 mt-1">
                            <span class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono">Table ${m.table} • ${m.division}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="text-xl font-black text-white mb-4">${p1} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-sm">vs</span> ${p2}</div>
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-4 bg-black/40 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 mb-4 shadow-inner">
                            <div class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">Adjust Final Score:</div>
                            <input type="number" id="live-s1-${id}" value="${s1}" class="w-14 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-2 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none text-lg">
                            <span class="text-slate-500 font-black">-</span>
                            <input type="number" id="live-s2-${id}" value="${s2}" class="w-14 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-2 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none text-lg">
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex gap-3">
                            <button onclick="window.forceFinishLive('${id}', '${p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="flex-1 bg-blue-600 hover:bg-blue-500 text-white font-bold py-2.5 rounded-lg text-sm transition-transform hover:scale-[1.02] shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(37,99,235,0.4)] flex items-center justify-center gap-2"><i class="fa-solid fa-flag-checkered"></i> Force Finish</button>
                            <button onclick="window.wipeLiveMatch('${id}')" class="bg-red-900/50 hover:bg-red-600 text-red-400 hover:text-white border border-red-500/30 font-bold py-2.5 px-4 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors" title="Wipe Error"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                } else if (m.match_status === "Scheduled" || !m.match_status) {
                    const formatVal = m.format_override || "Auto";
                    schedHtml += `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800/80 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shadow relative">
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-400 font-black uppercase tracking-widest mb-1 border-b border-white/5 pb-1 flex justify-between">
                            <span>Table ${m.table}</span><span class="text-blue-400">${m.division}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div class="font-bold text-white text-sm mt-2">${m.home_team} <br><span class="text-slate-500 text-xs font-normal">vs</span><br> ${m.away_team}</div>
                        <div class="mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-white/5">
                            <label class="block text-[9px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1">Match Format</label>
                            <select onchange="window.setFormatOverride('${id}', this.value)" class="w-full bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-slate-300 font-bold text-xs rounded py-2 px-2 focus:border-blue-500 outline-none">
                                <option value="Auto" ${formatVal === 'Auto' ? 'selected' : ''}>Auto-Detect</option>
                                <option value="2v2" ${formatVal === '2v2' ? 'selected' : ''}>Force 2v2 (5 Matches)</option>
                                <option value="3v3" ${formatVal === '3v3' ? 'selected' : ''}>Force 3v3 (11 Matches)</option>
                            </select>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }
            });
            
            if (liveList) liveList.innerHTML = liveHtml || '<div class="col-span-1 md:col-span-2 text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 rounded-xl bg-slate-800/30">No matches currently active.</div>';
            if (scheduledList) scheduledList.innerHTML = schedHtml || '<div class="col-span-1 md:col-span-3 text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 rounded-xl bg-slate-800/30">No scheduled matches pending.</div>';
        });

        window.forceFinishLive = async function(id, p1, p2) {
            const s1 = document.getElementById(`live-s1-${id}`).value; 
            const s2 = document.getElementById(`live-s2-${id}`).value;
            
            if (!confirm(`FORCE FINISH MATCH:\n\n${p1} vs ${p2}\nFinal Score: ${s1} - ${s2}\n\nProceed?`)) return;
            
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/admin/force_finish_live', { 
                    method: 'POST', 
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ id: id, s1: s1, s2: s2 }) 
                });
                const data = await res.json();
                if (data.success) alert("✅ Match forced finished!"); 
                else alert("❌ Error finishing match.");
            } catch(e) { 
                alert("Network Error"); 
            }
        };

        window.wipeLiveMatch = async function(id) {
            if (!confirm(`WIPE MATCH:\n\nAre you sure you want to completely erase this match?`)) return;
            try {
                const res = await fetch('/api/admin/wipe_live', { 
                    method: 'POST', 
                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                    body: JSON.stringify({ id: id }) 
                });
                const data = await res.json();
                if (data.success) alert("🗑️ Match wiped successfully!"); 
                else alert("❌ Error wiping match.");
            } catch(e) { 
                alert("Network Error"); 
            }
        };
    } catch(err) {
        console.warn("Firebase Live Connection skipped/failed. Check rules or CORS (harmless locally).");
    }
</script>

==> ./frontend/templates/Components/Admin/admin_scripts.html <==
<script>
    console.log("✅ Admin UI Script Loaded Successfully!");

    // ==========================================
    // AUTO LOGOUT TIMER (2 MINS INACTIVITY)
    // ==========================================
    const inactivityTime = function () {
        let time;
        window.onload = resetTimer;
        document.onmousemove = resetTimer;
        document.onkeypress = resetTimer;
        document.ontouchstart = resetTimer;
        document.onclick = resetTimer;

        function logout() {
            alert("You have been logged out due to 2 minutes of inactivity.");
            window.location.href = '/logout';
        }

        function resetTimer() {
            clearTimeout(time);
            time = setTimeout(logout, 120000); // 120000ms = 2 minutes
        }
    };
    inactivityTime();

    // ==========================================
    // UI NAVIGATION ENGINE
    // ==========================================
    window.setAdminCategory = function(catId) {
        ['ops', 'players', 'setup', 'comms', 'system'].forEach(c => {
            const btn = document.getElementById(`cat-${c}`);
            if (btn) { 
                btn.classList.remove('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-400'); 
                btn.classList.add('border-transparent', 'text-slate-500'); 
            }
            const sub = document.getElementById(`sub-${c}`);
            if (sub) sub.classList.add('hidden');
        });

        const targetBtn = document.getElementById(`cat-${catId}`);
        if (targetBtn) { 
            targetBtn.classList.remove('border-transparent', 'text-slate-500'); 
            targetBtn.classList.add('border-blue-500', 'text-blue-400'); 
        }
        
        const targetSub = document.getElementById(`sub-${catId}`);
        if (targetSub) targetSub.classList.remove('hidden');

        if (catId === 'ops') window.switchAdminTab('live');
        if (catId === 'players') window.switchAdminTab('players');
        if (catId === 'setup') window.switchAdminTab('schedules');
        if (catId === 'comms') window.switchAdminTab('notices');
        if (catId === 'system') window.switchAdminTab('audit');
    };

    window.switchAdminTab = function(tabId) {
        const allTabs = [
            'live', 'manual', 'history', 'date-errors', 'tournaments', 
            'players', 'diagnostics', 'schedules', 'team-editor', 'broadcast', 
            'sms-inbox', 'notices', 'community-mod', 'inbox-feedback', 'donations', 'audit', 'chat',
            'pending-accounts' 
        ];

        allTabs.forEach(t => {
            const section = document.getElementById(`admin-${t}`);
            if (section) section.classList.add('hidden');
            
            const btn = document.getElementById(`tab-btn-${t}`);
            if (btn) btn.className = "px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold text-slate-400 hover:text-white cursor-pointer whitespace-nowrap transition-colors";
        });
        
        const targetSection = document.getElementById(`admin-${tabId}`);
        if (targetSection) targetSection.classList.remove('hidden');
        
        const targetBtn = document.getElementById(`tab-btn-${tabId}`);
        if (targetBtn) targetBtn.className = "px-4 py-2 text-xs font-bold text-white bg-white/10 rounded-lg cursor-pointer whitespace-nowrap transition-colors";

        if (tabId === 'inbox-feedback') window.loadPendingReports();
        if (tabId === 'date-errors') window.loadDateErrors();
        if (tabId === 'notices') window.loadAdminNotices();
        if (tabId === 'chat') window.loadAdminChat();
        if (tabId === 'donations') window.loadDonations();
        if (tabId === 'sms-inbox') window.loadSmsInbox();
        if (tabId === 'community-mod') window.loadCommunityMod();
        if (tabId === 'team-editor') window.loadTeams();
        if (tabId === 'pending-accounts') window.loadPendingAccounts();
        
        if (tabId === 'schedules') window.loadSchedules();
        
        if (tabId === 'history') {
            const histDivFilter = document.getElementById('hist-div-filter');
            if (histDivFilter && histDivFilter.options.length <= 1) {
                fetch('/api/divisions').then(r => r.json()).then(divs => { divs.forEach(d => { histDivFilter.innerHTML += `<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`; }); });
            }
        }
        
        if (['players', 'diagnostics', 'manual'].includes(tabId) && playerDirectoryData.length === 0) window.loadPlayerDirectory();
        if (tabId === 'players') window.loadChaosConfig();
        
        if (tabId === 'diagnostics') {
            fetch('/api/admin/get_rating_scales').then(r => r.json()).then(d => {
                document.getElementById('math-k-win').value = d.k_win; 
                document.getElementById('math-k-loss').value = d.k_loss;
            });
        }
        
        if (tabId === 'audit') { window.loadAuditLogs(); window.loadAdminUsers(); window.loadTrafficStats(); }
    };

    window.forceRefresh = async function() {
        if (!confirm("Force the server to pull the latest data from the Master Google Sheet?")) return;
        const btn = document.querySelector('button[onclick="window.forceRefresh()"]');
        const originalHtml = btn ? btn.innerHTML : "FORCE REFRESH";
        if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> SYNCING...'; btn.disabled = true; }
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/refresh', { method: 'POST' });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) alert("✅ Sync triggered! Changes will appear momentarily."); else alert("❌ Sync failed.");
        } catch(e) { alert("❌ Network Error."); } finally { if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = originalHtml; btn.disabled = false; } }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // SMS BROADCASTING & CONTACT LIST ENGINE
    // ==========================================
    window.currentSmsContacts = [];

    window.copyContactList = async function(type) {
        const btn = document.getElementById(`btn-copy-${type}`);
        if(!btn) return;
        const origHTML = btn.innerHTML;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Fetching...';
        btn.disabled = true;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/contacts');
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);

            const textToCopy = type === 'emails' ? data.emails : data.phones;
            if (!textToCopy) {
                alert(`No ${type} found.`);
            } else {
                await navigator.clipboard.writeText(textToCopy);
                alert(`✅ Copied ${textToCopy.split(',').length} ${type} to clipboard!`);
            }
        } catch(e) {
            alert("Error: " + e.message);
        } finally {
            btn.innerHTML = origHTML;
            btn.disabled = false;
        }
    };

    window.verifySmsList = async function() {
        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-verify-sms');
        if(!btn) return;
        const origHTML = btn.innerHTML;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Loading...';
        btn.disabled = true;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/contacts');
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);

            window.currentSmsContacts = data.preview || [];
            if (window.currentSmsContacts.length === 0) {
                alert("No opted-in phone numbers found.");
                return;
            }

            const divs = new Set(window.currentSmsContacts.map(c => c.division));
            const filterSelect = document.getElementById('sms-div-filter');
            if(filterSelect) {
                filterSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="All">All Divisions</option>';
                divs.forEach(d => {
                    if(d) filterSelect.innerHTML += `<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`;
                });
            }

            window.currentSmsContacts.forEach(c => c.selected = true);
            const previewBox = document.getElementById('sms-preview-box');
            if(previewBox) previewBox.classList.remove('hidden');
            window.renderSmsPreviewList();
            
        } catch(e) {
            alert("Error: " + e.message);
        } finally {
            btn.innerHTML = origHTML;
            btn.disabled = false;
        }
    };

    window.renderSmsPreviewList = function() {
        const filterEl = document.getElementById('sms-div-filter');
        const filter = filterEl ? filterEl.value : 'All';
        const listEl = document.getElementById('preview-list');
        if(!listEl) return;
        
        let html = '';
        let visibleCount = 0;
        let selectedCount = 0;

        window.currentSmsContacts.forEach((c, idx) => {
            if (c.selected) selectedCount++;
            if (filter === 'All' || c.division === filter) {
                visibleCount++;
                html += `
                <div class="flex justify-between items-center bg-black/20 p-2 rounded border border-white/5">
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3">
                        <input type="checkbox" id="sms-cb-${idx}" ${c.selected ? 'checked' : ''} onchange="window.toggleSmsSelection(${idx}, this.checked)" class="w-4 h-4 rounded bg-slate-900 border-white/10 text-emerald-500 focus:ring-emerald-500">
                        <div>
                            <div class="font-bold text-white text-sm leading-tight">${c.name}</div>
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono">${c.phone}</div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-[10px] bg-slate-800 text-slate-400 px-2 py-0.5 rounded border border-white/10">${c.division}</div>
                </div>`;
            }
        });

        if (visibleCount === 0) {
            html = '<div class="text-center py-4 text-slate-500 italic text-xs">No players match this filter.</div>';
        }

        listEl.innerHTML = html;
        const countEl = document.getElementById('preview-count');
        if(countEl) countEl.innerText = selectedCount;
    };

    window.toggleSmsSelection = function(idx, isChecked) {
        if (window.currentSmsContacts[idx]) {
            window.currentSmsContacts[idx].selected = isChecked;
            const countEl = document.getElementById('preview-count');
            if(countEl) countEl.innerText = window.currentSmsContacts.filter(c => c.selected).length;
        }
    };

    window.filterSmsList = function() {
        window.renderSmsPreviewList();
    };

    window.toggleAllSms = function() {
        const filterEl = document.getElementById('sms-div-filter');
        const filter = filterEl ? filterEl.value : 'All';
        const visibleContacts = window.currentSmsContacts.filter(c => filter === 'All' || c.division === filter);
        const allChecked = visibleContacts.every(c => c.selected);
        
        visibleContacts.forEach(c => c.selected = !allChecked);
        window.renderSmsPreviewList();
    };

    window.sendSmsBroadcast = async function() {
        const msgInput = document.getElementById('broadcast-input');
        if(!msgInput) return alert("Message box not found.");
        const msg = msgInput.value.trim();
        if (!msg) return alert("Please enter a custom message.");
        
        const selectedPhones = window.currentSmsContacts.filter(c => c.selected).map(c => c.phone);
        if (selectedPhones.length === 0) return alert("Please select at least one recipient first using the verification tool.");

        if (!confirm(`You are about to send an SMS to ${selectedPhones.length} players.\n\nProceed?`)) return;

        const btn = document.getElementById('btn-send-sms');
        const origHTML = btn.innerHTML;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> SENDING...';
        btn.disabled = true;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/send_sms', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ message: msg, phones: selectedPhones })
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                alert("✅ " + data.message);
                msgInput.value = '';
                msgInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input'));
                window.currentSmsContacts = [];
                const previewBox = document.getElementById('sms-preview-box');
                if(previewBox) previewBox.classList.add('hidden');
            } else {
                alert("❌ Failed: " + data.error);
            }
        } catch(e) {
            alert("Network error while sending SMS.");
        } finally {
            btn.innerHTML = origHTML;
            btn.disabled = false;
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // CHAOS CONFIG
    // ==========================================
    window.loadChaosConfig = async function() {
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/chaos_config');
            const data = await res.json();
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    // ==========================================
    // GLICKO SIMULATOR & MATH MULTIPLIERS
    // ==========================================
    window.runDiagnostics = async function() {
        const p1 = document.getElementById('diag-p1-search').value; 
        const p2 = document.getElementById('diag-p2-search').value; 
        const s1 = document.getElementById('diag-s1').value; 
        const s2 = document.getElementById('diag-s2').value;
        const resultsBox = document.getElementById('diag-results'); 
        const btn = document.getElementById('diag-btn');
        
        if(!p1 || !p2) return alert("Please select both players.");
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> Calculating...';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/glicko_calc', { 
                method: 'POST', 
                headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, 
                body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, s1: s1, s2: s2 }) 
            });
            const d = await res.json();
            if(d.success) {
                const math = d.data;
                const renderPlayerMath = (pData) => {
                    const deltaColor = pData.delta > 0 ? "text-emerald-400" : "text-red-400";
                    const deltaSign = pData.delta > 0 ? "+" : "";
                    const rdColor = pData.rd_delta > 0 ? "text-red-400" : "text-emerald-400"; // RD going down is good
                    const rdSign = pData.rd_delta > 0 ? "+" : "";

                    return `
                    <div class="bg-slate-800 p-5 rounded-xl border border-white/5 relative">
                        <div class="font-black text-white text-lg mb-4 border-b border-white/10 pb-2">${pData.name}</div>
                        <div class="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                            <div>
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1">Current Rating</div>
                                <div class="text-xl font-mono text-white">${Math.round(pData.old_rating)}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500 mb-1">Deviation (RD)</div>
                                <div class="text-xl font-mono text-slate-400">±${Math.round(pData.old_rd)}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-white/10 flex flex-col gap-2 bg-black/20 p-3 rounded-lg">
                            <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500">Rating Shift</div>
                                <div class="text-lg font-black font-mono ${deltaColor}">${deltaSign}${pData.delta.toFixed(1)} pts</div>
                            </div>
                            <div class="flex justify-between items-center">
                                <div class="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-slate-500">RD Shift</div>
                                <div class="text-sm font-black font-mono ${rdColor}">${rdSign}${pData.rd_delta.toFixed(1)}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex justify-between items-center mt-3 pt-3 border-t border-white/5">
                            <span class="text-[10px] uppercase text-slate-500 font-bold">New Stats: </span>
                            <span class="text-white font-mono font-bold">${Math.round(pData.new_rating)} <span class="text-slate-400 text-xs ml-1">±${Math.round(pData.new_rd)}</span></span>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                };
                resultsBox.innerHTML = `<div class="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">${renderPlayerMath(math.p1)}${renderPlayerMath(math.p2)}</div>`;
                resultsBox.classList.remove('hidden');
            }
        } catch(e) { 
            alert("Network Error"); 
        } finally { 
            btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-microchip"></i> Run Simulation'; 
        }
    };

    window.saveMathMultipliers = async function() {
        const kWin = document.getElementById('math-k-win').value;
        const kLoss = document.getElementById('math-k-loss').value;
        if(!confirm(`Are you sure you want to change the global rating modifiers?\n\nK-Win: ${kWin}\nK-Loss: ${kLoss}\n\nThis will trigger a full history recalculation.`)) return;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/set_rating_scales', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
                body: JSON.stringify({k_win: kWin, k_loss: kLoss})
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if(data.success) {
                alert("✅ Modifiers saved! The server will now recalculate all ratings.");
                window.forceRefresh();
            } else alert("❌ Failed to save modifiers.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error."); }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // PLAYER SEARCH UTILITIES
    // ==========================================
    let playerDirectoryData = [];
    
    window.loadPlayerDirectory = async function() { 
        try { const res = await fetch('/api/admin/player_directory'); playerDirectoryData = await res.json(); } catch(e) {} 
    };

    function attachPlayerSearch(inputId, suggId, hiddenId = null) {
        const input = document.getElementById(inputId); const sugg = document.getElementById(suggId);
        if (!input || !sugg) return;
        
        input.addEventListener('input', (e) => {
            const q = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
            if (q.length < 1) { sugg.classList.add('hidden'); return; }
            
            const matches = playerDirectoryData.filter(p => p.name.toLowerCase().includes(q));
            if (matches.length === 0) { sugg.innerHTML = '<div class="px-3 py-2 text-slate-400 text-xs italic">No players found</div>'; sugg.classList.remove('hidden'); return; }
            
            sugg.innerHTML = matches.slice(0, 8).map(p => `
                <div class="px-4 py-2 hover:bg-blue-600/30 cursor-pointer text-sm text-white font-bold border-b border-white/5" 
                     onclick="document.getElementById('${inputId}').value = '${p.name.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}'; ${hiddenId ? `document.getElementById('${hiddenId}').value = '${p.id}';` : ''} document.getElementById('${suggId}').classList.add('hidden'); ${hiddenId === 'override-id' ? `window.fetchRatingContext('${p.id}');` : ''}">
                    ${p.name} <span class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono ml-2">${p.id}</span>
                </div>
            `).join('');
            sugg.classList.remove('hidden');
        });
        
        document.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target !== input && e.target !== sugg) sugg.classList.add('hidden'); });
    }

    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
        window.setAdminCategory('ops'); 
        attachPlayerSearch('override-search', 'override-suggestions', 'override-id');
        attachPlayerSearch('merge-bad-search', 'merge-bad-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('merge-good-search', 'merge-good-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('diag-p1-search', 'diag-p1-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('diag-p2-search', 'diag-p2-suggestions');
        attachPlayerSearch('manual-p1', 'sugg-p1');
        attachPlayerSearch('manual-p2', 'sugg-p2');
        attachPlayerSearch('profile-edit-search', 'profile-edit-sugg');

        const searchInput = document.getElementById('profile-edit-search');
        if(searchInput) {
            searchInput.addEventListener('blur', () => {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    const playerName = searchInput.value.trim();
                    if(playerName) window.loadProfileForEditing(playerName);
                }, 200); 
            });
        }
    });

    // ==========================================
    // PLAYER PROFILE EDITOR
    // ==========================================
    window.loadProfileForEditing = async function(playerName) {
        const rcInput = document.getElementById('profile-rc-id');
        const saveBtn = document.getElementById('profile-save-btn');
        rcInput.disabled = true; saveBtn.disabled = true; rcInput.value = "Loading...";

        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/player_profile/${encodeURIComponent(playerName)}`);
            const data = await res.json();
            rcInput.value = data.ratings_central_id || '';
            rcInput.disabled = false; saveBtn.disabled = false;
        } catch(e) {
            rcInput.value = ""; alert("Error loading player profile.");
        }
    };

    window.savePlayerProfile = async function() {
        const playerName = document.getElementById('profile-edit-search').value.trim();
        const rcId = document.getElementById('profile-rc-id').value.trim();
        if(!playerName) return alert("Please select a player first.");
        
        const btn = document.getElementById('profile-save-btn'); const origText = btn.innerHTML;
        btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> SAVING...'; btn.disabled = true;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/update_player_profile', {
                method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
                body: JSON.stringify({ player_name: playerName, ratings_central_id: rcId })
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if(data.success) alert(`✅ Profile updated successfully!`); else alert("❌ Failed to update profile.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error"); } finally { btn.innerHTML = origText; btn.disabled = false; }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // ACCOUNT LINKING APPROVALS
    // ==========================================
    window.loadPendingAccounts = async function() {
        const list = document.getElementById('pendingAccountsList'); if (!list) return;
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl text-indigo-500"></i></div>';
        if (playerDirectoryData.length === 0) await window.loadPlayerDirectory();

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/pending_accounts'); const data = await res.json();
            if (data.length === 0) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-xl">Awesome! No pending accounts to approve.</div>'; return; }

            let html = '';
            data.forEach(a => {
                html += `
                <div class="bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 shadow-lg mb-3">
                    <div>
                        <div class="font-bold text-white text-lg">${a.name}</div>
                        <div class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono">${a.email} • DOB: ${a.dob}</div>
                        <div class="text-[10px] text-slate-500 font-mono mt-1">UID: ${a.uid}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 bg-black/30 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 w-full md:w-auto">
                        <div class="relative w-full md:w-64">
                            <input type="text" id="link-search-${a.uid}" placeholder="Link to official player..." class="w-full bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-xs outline-none focus:border-indigo-500" autocomplete="off" value="${a.name}">
                            <div id="link-sugg-${a.uid}" class="absolute z-50 left-0 right-0 top-full mt-1 bg-slate-700 rounded shadow-xl hidden border border-white/10 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar"></div>
                        </div>
                        <button onclick="window.linkAccount('${a.uid}')" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white font-bold py-2.5 px-4 rounded-lg text-xs transition shadow-lg whitespace-nowrap"><i class="fa-solid fa-link mr-1"></i> Approve</button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
            data.forEach(a => { attachPlayerSearch(`link-search-${a.uid}`, `link-sugg-${a.uid}`); });
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.linkAccount = async function(uid) {
        const playerName = document.getElementById(`link-search-${uid}`).value;
        if (!playerName) return alert("Please select an official player name to link.");
        if (!confirm(`Link UID ${uid} to ${playerName}?`)) return;

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/link_account', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ uid: uid, player_name: playerName }) });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { alert("✅ Account approved!"); window.loadPendingAccounts(); } else alert("❌ Failed to link account.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error"); }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // SCHEDULE / FIXTURE MANAGER
    // ==========================================
    window.upcomingSchedules = [];

    window.loadSchedules = async function() {
        const listEl = document.getElementById('schedules-list');
        if(!listEl) return;
        listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl text-red-500"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/upcoming_schedules');
            window.upcomingSchedules = await res.json();
            
            const divs = new Set(window.upcomingSchedules.map(s => s.division));
            const filterEl = document.getElementById('schedule-div-filter');
            if (filterEl && filterEl.options.length <= 1) {
                divs.forEach(d => {
                    if(d) filterEl.innerHTML += `<option value="${d}">${d}</option>`;
                });
            }
            window.renderSchedules();
        } catch(e) { 
            listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-red-500 text-xs text-center py-4">Failed to load schedules.</div>'; 
        }
    };

    window.renderSchedules = function() {
        const filterObj = document.getElementById('schedule-div-filter');
        const filter = filterObj ? filterObj.value : 'All';
        const listEl = document.getElementById('schedules-list');
        if(!listEl) return;
        
        let filtered = window.upcomingSchedules;
        if (filter !== 'All') {
            filtered = filtered.filter(s => s.division === filter);
        }
        
        if (filtered.length === 0) {
            listEl.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 rounded-xl bg-black/20">No matches extracted yet. Upload a PDF first.</div>';
            return;
        }
        
        let html = '';
        filtered.forEach(s => {
            html += `
            <div class="bg-black/30 border border-white/5 p-4 rounded-lg flex justify-between items-center group transition-colors hover:bg-slate-800">
                <div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1.5">
                        <span class="bg-blue-900/30 text-blue-400 border border-blue-500/20 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded font-bold uppercase tracking-widest">${s.division}</span>
                        <span class="text-xs text-slate-400 font-mono"><i class="fa-regular fa-calendar mr-1"></i>${s.date_text}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="text-sm font-black text-white">${s.home_team} <span class="text-slate-500 text-xs font-normal mx-2 text-[10px] uppercase">vs</span> ${s.away_team}</div>
                </div>
                <button onclick="window.deleteSchedule('${s.id}')" title="Delete Duplicate Match" class="text-red-500 hover:text-white bg-red-900/20 hover:bg-red-600 border border-red-500/20 rounded px-3 py-2 transition opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 shadow"><i class="fa-solid fa-trash"></i></button>
            </div>`;
        });
        listEl.innerHTML = html;
    };

    window.deleteSchedule = async function(id) {
        if(!confirm("Are you sure you want to delete this match from the schedule?")) return;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/delete_schedule', {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
                body: JSON.stringify({schedule_id: id})
            });
            const data = await res.json();
            if(data.success) {
                window.loadSchedules();
            } else alert("Failed to delete schedule.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error"); }
    };

    window.uploadPdfSchedule = async function(event) {
        if (event) event.preventDefault();
        
        const fileInput = document.getElementById('pdf-file-upload'); 
        const seasonInput = document.getElementById('pdf-season');
        const divInput = document.getElementById('pdf-division');
        
        if (!fileInput || !fileInput.files || fileInput.files.length === 0) {
            return alert("Please select a PDF file first. If you did, hard refresh the page (Cmd+Shift+R) to clear your cache.");
        }
        
        const season = seasonInput ? seasonInput.value : 'Unknown Season';
        const division = divInput ? divInput.value : 'Unknown Division';

        const formData = new FormData();
        formData.append('pdf', fileInput.files[0]);
        formData.append('season', season);
        formData.append('division', division);

        const btn = document.getElementById('pdf-upload-btn');
        const origHtml = btn ? btn.innerHTML : 'EXTRACT MATCHUPS';
        if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> PARSING...'; btn.disabled = true; }

        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/upload_schedule', { method: 'POST', body: formData });
            const data = await res.json();
            
            if (data.success) {
                alert(`✅ Extraction Complete!\n\nFound ${data.teams_found} teams and ${data.matches_found} matchups.`);
                window.loadSchedules();
            } else alert("❌ Failed to parse PDF: " + data.error);
        } catch(e) {
            alert("❌ Network error while uploading PDF.");
        } finally {
            if (btn) { btn.innerHTML = origHtml; btn.disabled = false; }
            if (fileInput) fileInput.value = '';
        }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MANUAL MATCH & HISTORY
    // ==========================================
    window.submitManualMatch = async function() {
        const p1 = document.getElementById('manual-p1').value; const p2 = document.getElementById('manual-p2').value;
        const date = document.getElementById('manual-date').value; const scores = document.getElementById('manual-scores').value;
        if (!p1 || !p2 || !date) return alert("Player 1, Player 2, and Date are required.");
        if (!confirm(`Create match record?\n\n${p1} vs ${p2}\nDate: ${date}`)) return;
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/manual_match', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, date: date, scores: scores }) });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { alert(`✅ Match injected successfully!`); document.getElementById('manual-p1').value = ''; document.getElementById('manual-p2').value = ''; document.getElementById('manual-scores').value = ''; } 
            else alert("❌ Error injecting match.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network error."); }
    };

    window.searchHistory = async function() {
        const q = document.getElementById('history-search').value.trim(); 
        const divFilterObj = document.getElementById('hist-div-filter');
        const sourceFilterObj = document.getElementById('hist-source-filter');
        const divFilter = divFilterObj ? divFilterObj.value : 'All'; const sourceFilter = sourceFilterObj ? sourceFilterObj.value : 'All';
        const list = document.getElementById('historyList'); 
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-indigo-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        
        try {
            const res = await fetch(`/api/admin/history?q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}&source=${encodeURIComponent(sourceFilter)}`); 
            let matches = await res.json();
            if (divFilter !== 'All') matches = matches.filter(m => m.division.toLowerCase() === divFilter.toLowerCase());
            
            if (matches.length === 0) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic">No matches found.</div>'; return; }
            
            let html = '';
            matches.forEach(m => {
                let gameHistoryHtml = m.game_history ? `<div class="mt-3 bg-black/30 p-2 rounded border border-white/5 text-center text-xs font-mono text-slate-300">Set Scores: ${m.game_history}</div>` : (m.rich_stats && m.rich_stats.total_duration ? `<div class="mt-3 bg-blue-900/20 p-2 rounded border border-blue-500/20 text-center text-xs text-blue-300"><i class="fa-solid fa-tablet-screen-button"></i> iPad Match • Duration: ${m.rich_stats.total_duration}</div>` : '');
                const sourceBadge = m.source === 'Spreadsheet' ? `<span class="bg-green-900/30 text-green-400 border border-green-500/20 text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner"><i class="fa-solid fa-file-excel mr-1"></i>Sheet</span>` : `<span class="bg-blue-900/30 text-blue-400 border border-blue-500/20 text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded shadow-inner"><i class="fa-solid fa-tablet mr-1"></i>App</span>`;

                html += `
                <div class="bg-black/30 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 mb-3 flex flex-col hover:bg-slate-800 transition-colors">
                    <div class="flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 w-full">
                        <div class="flex-1 w-full">
                            <div class="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                                <span class="bg-slate-800 text-slate-300 px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-[10px] font-mono border border-white/10">ID: ${m.match_id || 'N/A'}</span>
                                <span class="bg-indigo-900/30 text-indigo-400 border border-indigo-500/20 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded uppercase font-bold tracking-widest">${m.division}</span>
                                ${sourceBadge}
                            </div>
                            <div class="text-lg font-black text-white">${m.p1} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-sm">vs</span> ${m.p2}</div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-slate-900/80 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/10 w-full md:w-auto shrink-0">
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-14"><span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Score 1</span><input type="number" id="s1-${m.id}" value="${m.s1}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm"></div>
                            <span class="text-slate-600 font-black mt-3">-</span>
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-14"><span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Score 2</span><input type="number" id="s2-${m.id}" value="${m.s2}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm"></div>
                            <div class="flex flex-col w-28 ml-2"><span class="text-[8px] text-slate-500 uppercase font-bold mb-1 text-center">Date</span><input type="text" id="date-${m.id}" value="${m.date}" class="w-full bg-slate-800 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1.5 focus:border-indigo-500 outline-none text-sm"></div>
                            <div class="flex flex-col gap-1 ml-2 mt-4">
                                <button onclick="window.adminSaveHistoryEdit('${m.p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.date}', '${m.id}')" class="bg-indigo-600 hover:bg-indigo-500 text-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition shadow-lg flex items-center justify-center"><i class="fa-solid fa-floppy-disk"></i></button>
                                <button onclick="document.getElementById('data-${m.match_id}').classList.toggle('hidden')" class="bg-slate-700 hover:bg-slate-600 text-white px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg transition shadow-lg flex items-center justify-center" title="View Match Data"><i class="fa-solid fa-chart-simple"></i></button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                    <div id="data-${m.match_id}" class="hidden w-full mt-4 bg-black/40 border border-white/5 rounded-xl p-4 flex-col gap-3">
                        <div class="mt-4 pt-3 border-t border-white/10 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-center justify-between gap-3">
                            <div class="text-[10px] text-yellow-500 font-bold uppercase tracking-widest"><i class="fa-solid fa-wrench mr-1"></i> Override Point Changes</div>
                            <div class="flex items-center gap-2">
                                <input type="number" step="0.1" id="override-p1-${m.match_id}" placeholder="${m.p1} pts" class="w-24 bg-black/40 border border-white/10 text-white text-center rounded py-1.5 text-xs focus:ring-1 focus:ring-yellow-500 outline-none" value="${m.p1_delta ? Math.round(m.p1_delta) : ''}">
                                <input type="number" step="0.1" id="override-p2-${m.match_id}" placeholder="${m.p2} pts" class="w-24 bg-black/40 border border-white/10 text-white text-center rounded py-1.5 text-xs focus:ring-1 focus:ring-yellow-500 outline-none" value="${m.p2_delta ? Math.round(m.p2_delta) : ''}">
                                <button onclick="window.saveDeltaOverride('${m.match_id}', '${m.p1.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${m.p2.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}')" class="bg-yellow-600 hover:bg-yellow-500 text-black font-black px-3 py-1.5 rounded text-xs transition shadow-lg">SAVE</button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            list.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.saveDeltaOverride = async function(matchId, p1, p2) {
        const p1Delta = document.getElementById(`override-p1-${matchId}`).value; const p2Delta = document.getElementById(`override-p2-${matchId}`).value;
        if (!p1Delta || !p2Delta) return alert("Please enter point changes for both players.");
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/override_deltas', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ match_id: matchId, p1_delta: p1Delta, p2_delta: p2Delta }) });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { alert("✅ Point overrides saved!"); window.searchHistory(); } else alert("❌ Failed to save.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error"); }
    };

    window.adminSaveHistoryEdit = async function(p1, p2, oldDate, id) {
        const s1 = document.getElementById(`s1-${id}`).value; const s2 = document.getElementById(`s2-${id}`).value; const newDate = document.getElementById(`date-${id}`).value;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/update_match', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ p1: p1, p2: p2, date: oldDate, s1: s1, s2: s2, new_date: newDate }) });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) alert("✅ Update locked in!"); else alert("❌ Failed to update match.");
        } catch(e) { alert("Network Error"); }
    };

    // ==========================================
    // MISSING DATE FIXER
    // ==========================================
    window.loadDateErrors = async function() {
        const dList = document.getElementById('dateErrorsList'); const dBadge = document.getElementById('date-badge');
        if (!dList) return; dList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-center py-10 text-orange-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-spinner fa-spin text-2xl"></i></div>';
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/date_errors'); const errors = await res.json();
            if (dBadge) { dBadge.innerText = errors.length; errors.length > 0 ? dBadge.classList.remove('hidden') : dBadge.classList.add('hidden'); }
            if (errors.length === 0) { dList.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-600 text-center py-10 italic border border-white/5 bg-slate-800/30 rounded-xl">Awesome! No missing dates found.</div>'; return; }
            let html = "";
            errors.forEach(m => {
                html += `
                <div id="date-card-${m.id}" class="date-card bg-slate-800 p-4 rounded-xl border border-white/5 flex flex-col md:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-4 shadow-lg mb-3" data-season="${m.season}" data-div="${m.division}" data-week="${m.week}">
                    <div class="flex-1 w-full"><div class="font-black text-white text-lg">${m.home_players[0]} <span class="text-slate-500 mx-2 text-sm">vs</span> ${m.away_players[0]}</div></div>
                    <div class="flex items-center gap-3 bg-black/30 p-3 rounded-xl border border-white/5 shrink-0">
                        <div class="flex flex-col"><input type="text" id="fix-date-${m.id}" placeholder="e.g. 14/02/2026" class="w-28 bg-slate-900 border border-white/10 text-white font-bold font-mono text-center rounded py-1 focus:border-orange-500 focus:outline-none text-xs"></div>
                        <button onclick="window.adminBulkDateFix('${m.season}', '${m.division}', '${m.week}', '${m.id}', this)" class="bg-orange-600 hover:bg-orange-500 text-white font-bold py-2 px-4 rounded text-xs transition-transform shadow mt-1">FIX</button>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            });
            dList.innerHTML = html;
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.adminBulkDateFix = async function(season, division, week, id, btnElement) {
        const newDate = document.getElementById(`fix-date-${id}`).value;
        try {
            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/bulk_fix_date', { method: 'POST', headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }, body: JSON.stringify({ season: season, division: division, week: week, date: newDate }) });
            const data = await res.json();
            if (data.success) { setTimeout(() => document.getElementById(`date-card-${id}`).remove(), 300); }
        } catch(e) {}
    };

    window.loadDonations = async function() {

            const res = await fetch('/api/admin/donations'); const data = await res.json();
            if (data.length === 0) { list.innerHTML = '<div class="text-slate-500 text-center py-10 italic">No donations recorded yet.</div>'; return; }
            let html = '';
            data.forEach(d => {
                html += `<div class="bg-black/30 p-4 rounded-xl border border-emerald-500/20 flex justify-between items-center transition-colors hover:bg-slate-800"><div><div class="font-bold text-white text-lg">${d.name}</div></div><div class="text-2xl font-black text-emerald-400 font-mono">$${d.amount.toFixed(2)}</div></div>`;
